The supplementation of awards allows arbitral tribunals to render additional awards for claims that were presented but omitted in the original award, thereby preventing challenges based on infra petita grounds under annulment proceedings.

在国际仲裁领域，解决诉讼程序中提出的所有索赔以确保仲裁裁决的完整性和可执行性至关重要。裁决的补充允许仲裁庭对原裁决中提出但遗漏的索赔作出额外裁决，从而防止在撤销程序下基于以下理由提出质疑。

UNCITRAL Model Law - Article 33(3)

Article 33(3) of the UNCITRAL Model Law permits an arbitral tribunal to make an additional award as to any claims that were presented during the arbitral proceedings but omitted from the final award. This supplementation must be carried out within a 30-day limit unless the parties have expressly agreed otherwise.

《贸易法委员会示范法》第 33 条第(3)款允许仲裁庭对仲裁程序期间提出但最终裁决中遗漏的任何索赔作出附加裁决。除非双方另有明确约定，该补充必须在 30 天内进行。

The mechanism under Article 33(3) serves to prevent infra petita challenges during annulment proceedings under Article V(1)(C) of the New York Convention. Such challenges arise when an award fails to address claims that were presented, leading to potential grounds for partial annulment or refusal of enforcement. It is noteworthy that tribunals are not required to expressly address every part of a claim, as implied rejection or acceptance is permissible.

第 33 条第(3)款规定的机制旨在防止《纽约公约》第五条第(1)(C)款规定的废止程序中出现以下质疑。当裁决未能解决所提出的索赔时，就会出现此类挑战，从而导致部分废止或拒绝执行的潜在理由。值得注意的是，仲裁庭不需要明确处理索赔的每个部分，因为暗示拒绝或接受是允许的。

Institutional Rules Allowing Additional Awards

Numerous institutional arbitration rules also recognize the provision for supplementary awards:

许多机构仲裁规则也承认补充裁决的规定：

  • SIAC Rules 2016 : Rule 33(3) explicitly allows the making of additional awards. SIAC 规则 2016 ：第 33(3) 条明确允许作出额外裁决。
  • HKIAC Rules 2013 : Article 39 authorizes supplementary awards for omitted claims. HKIAC 规则 2013 ：第 39 条授权对遗漏索赔进行补充裁决。
  • VIAC Arbitration Rules 2013 : Article 39 provides for the same. VIAC 仲裁规则 2013 ：第 39 条有相同规定。
  • CEPANI Rules 2013 : Article 1715 §3 covers the procedure for additional awards. 2013 年 CEPANI 规则：第 1715 条第 3 条涵盖了额外奖励的程序。
  • ICC Rules 2012 : Although silent on the matter, supplemental awards are permitted if authorized under the Lex Arbitri (the law of the country where the arbitration is seated). 2012 年国际商会规则：虽然没有提及此事，但如果根据仲裁法（仲裁所在地国家的法律）授权，则允许补充裁决。

By integrating these mechanisms and rules, arbitration frameworks ensure that all presented claims are adjudicated, maintaining the award’s integrity and enforceability. This underscores the tribunals’ adaptability and focus on delivering comprehensive justice within the arbitration process.

通过整合这些机制和规则，仲裁框架可确保所有提出的索赔都得到裁决，从而保持裁决的完整性和可执行性。这凸显了仲裁庭的适应性以及对在仲裁过程中实现全面正义的关注。

Post-Award Relief in International Arbitration 国际仲裁中的裁决后救济

Post-award relief in international arbitration encompasses various mechanisms parties can use to address concerns with the arbitral award. These mechanisms ensure fairness and integrity in the arbitration process and provide parties with options to challenge, revise, or even revoke awards under certain conditions.

国际仲裁中的裁决后救济包括当事人可以用来解决对仲裁裁决的担忧的各种机制。这些机制确保了仲裁过程的公平性和完整性，并为当事人提供了在某些条件下质疑、修改甚至撤销裁决的选择。

Remission of an Award to the Arbitral Tribunal 向仲裁庭免除裁决

One significant post-award relief mechanism is the remission of an award to the arbitral tribunal. When an application to annul an award is filed, there may be a possibility to remit the award back to the tribunal for reconsideration. This can address procedural or substantive issues identified during the annulment process, providing a pathway for rectification.

一项重要的裁决后救济机制是将裁决免除给仲裁庭。当提出撤销裁决的申请时，可能有可能将裁决退回仲裁庭重新审议。这可以解决撤销过程中发现的程序性或实质性问题，提供纠正途径。

Revocation or Revision of Fraudulently Obtained Awards 撤销或修改以欺骗手段获得的裁决

In instances where an award is obtained through fraudulent means or comparable actions, parties can seek to have the award revoked or revised. This ensures that the arbitration process remains equitable and that awards reflect true and fair resolutions of the disputes.

如果通过欺诈手段或类似行为获得裁决，当事人可以寻求撤销或修改裁决。这确保了仲裁过程保持公平，并且裁决反映了争议的真实和公平的解决方案。

Institutional Appeals from International Arbitral Awards 国际仲裁裁决的机构上诉

While most institutional arbitration rules do not offer grounds for internal challenges within the arbitral procedure, leaving parties to pursue setting aside awards through judicial avenues, there are notable exceptions:

虽然大多数机构仲裁规则没有为仲裁程序中的内部质疑提供理由，使当事人可以通过司法途径寻求撤销裁决，但也有一些值得注意的例外：

  • ICSID Convention : ICSID 公约：
    • Article 52(1) provides for the annulment of awards by an Ad Hoc Committee, offering a structured method for challenging awards within the ICSID framework. 第 52(1) 条规定由特设委员会撤销裁决，为在 ICSID 框架内质疑裁决提供了结构化方法。
  • GAFTA Rules : 大亚自由贸易区规则：
    • Article 10(1) allows for appeals to a standing board of appeal, providing another layer of review within the arbitral institution. 第 10(1) 条允许向常设上诉委员会提出上诉，从而在仲裁机构内提供另一层审查。

These provisions highlight how specific institutional rules have created avenues for post-award relief, ensuring that arbitral decisions can be revisited in exceptional cases.

这些条款强调了具体的制度规则如何为裁决后救济创造途径，确保在特殊情况下可以重新审视仲裁决定。

Post-award relief mechanisms such as remission, revocation, and institutional appeals serve critical roles in maintaining the legitimacy and reliability of international arbitration. While the general trend is towards limiting internal challenges within arbitration institutions, specific frameworks like the ICSID Convention and GAFTA Rules offer structured processes for addressing grievances post-award. These mechanisms ensure that arbitration remains a robust, fair, and trustworthy method of dispute resolution on an international scale.

减免、撤销和机构上诉等裁决后救济机制在维护国际仲裁的合法性和可靠性方面发挥着关键作用。虽然总体趋势是限制仲裁机构内部的挑战，但《ICSID 公约》和《GAFTA 规则》等具体框架提供了解决裁决后申诉的结构化流程。这些机制确保仲裁在国际范围内仍然是一种稳健、公平和值得信赖的争议解决方法。

撤销仲裁裁决

The annulment of arbitral awards is a critical facet of international arbitration, emphasizing the need for efficiency and the preservation of the finality inherent in arbitration. It is widely recognized that the review and potential annulment of arbitration awards should be limited and only possible under exceptional circumstances, as highlighted by the European Court of Justice.

撤销仲裁裁决是国际仲裁的一个关键方面，强调了效率和维护仲裁固有的终局性的需要。正如欧洲法院所强调的那样，人们普遍认为，仲裁裁决的审查和可能的撤销应该受到限制，并且只有在特殊情况下才可能进行。

管辖范围和纽约公约 Jurisdictional Limits and the New York Convention

The New York Convention significantly influences where annulment actions can be brought, primarily restricting them to:

《纽约公约》极大地影响了可以提起无效诉讼的地点，主要将其限制为：

  1. The jurisdiction where the award was made. 作出裁决的司法管辖区。
  2. The jurisdiction under whose law the award was made. 裁决所依据的司法管辖区的法律。

Article V(1)(e) of the New York Convention implies these limitations, which facilitate the Convention’s objectives by preventing the circumvention of its narrow grounds for non-recognition. This avoids the dilution of the Convention’s effectiveness by constraining annulment to jurisdictions closely linked to the arbitration.

《纽约公约》第五条第(1)款(e)项隐含了这些限制，通过防止规避其狭隘的不承认理由，促进了《公约》的目标的实现。这避免了因将废除限制在与仲裁密切相关的司法管辖区而削弱公约的效力。

国家法规和领土方法 National Statutes and Territorial Approach

Most national laws reflect a territorial approach, limiting annulment actions to awards made within their jurisdiction. For instance:

大多数国家法律都体现了地域性做法，将撤销诉讼限制在其管辖范围内作出的裁决。例如：

  • UNCITRAL Model Law : Local courts cannot annul awards made outside the national territory. 贸易法委员会示范法：地方法院不能撤销在国家领土之外作出的裁决。
  • English Arbitration Act : Annulment is only possible if the arbitration seat is in England, unless parties agree otherwise. 英国仲裁法：只有当仲裁地位于英格兰时才可能撤销，除非双方另有约定。
  • U.S. Federal Arbitration Act : Annulment is limited to awards made within the United States. 美国联邦仲裁法：撤销仅限于在美国境内作出的裁决。

撤销的理由 Grounds for Annulment

Several grounds for annulment are recognized under both the UNCITRAL Model Law and the New York Convention, including:

《贸易法委员会示范法》和《纽约公约》均承认撤销的若干理由，包括：

  • Lack of Valid Arbitration Agreement : Ensuring the parties’ consent. 缺乏有效的仲裁协议：确保当事人同意。
  • Excess of Authority : Arbitrators exceeding their mandate. 越权：仲裁员超越其职权范围。
  • Denial of Opportunity to Present the Case : Fundamental procedural fairness. 拒绝陈述案件的机会：基本的程序公平。
  • Awards Contrary to Public Policy : Protecting essential national norms. 违反公共政策的裁决：保护基本国家规范。
  • Disputes Not Capable of Settlement by Arbitration : Reflecting core legal principles. 无法通过仲裁解决的争议：反映核心法律原则。
  • Bias and Arbitrator Misconduct : Ensuring arbitrator impartiality and integrity. 偏见和仲裁员不当行为：确保仲裁员的公正性和诚信。
  • Failure to Comply with Agreed Procedures : Adhering to procedural fairness. 不遵守商定程序：坚持程序公正。
  • Failure to Comply with Lex Arbitri : Compliance with the governing arbitration law. 不遵守仲裁法：遵守适用的仲裁法。

实质性审查和形式缺陷 Substantive Review and Formal Defects

  • While the trend is away from judicial review of the merits, some jurisdictions still allow it, including England, Ireland, China, and others. 尽管这种趋势已经不再对案情进行司法审查，但一些司法管辖区仍然允许这样做，包括英格兰、爱尔兰、中国等。
  • Formal defects such as internally contradictory awards and failure to comply with formal requirements can also be grounds for annulment as seen in the Belgian Judicial Code and the English Arbitration Act. 正如《比利时司法法典》和《英国仲裁法》中所见，形式上的缺陷，例如裁决内部矛盾和不遵守形式要求，也可以成为撤销裁决的理由。

The framework set by international conventions and national statutes strives to balance between respecting the finality of arbitral awards and safeguarding essential legal principles, thereby ensuring arbitration remains an effective and reliable means of dispute resolution.

国际公约和国家法规制定的框架力求在尊重仲裁裁决的终局性和维护基本法律原则之间取得平衡，从而确保仲裁仍然是有效、可靠的争议解决方式。

Agreements Waiving the Right to Seek Annulment of International Awards 放弃寻求撤销国际裁决权利的协议

In the realm of international arbitration, the finality of an arbitral award is a crucial advantage. However, parties sometimes seek to further cement this finality by agreeing to waive their right to seek annulment of the award. These agreements and their validity vary significantly across different jurisdictions and legal traditions.

在国际仲裁领域，仲裁裁决的终局性是一个至关重要的优势。然而，当事人有时会同意放弃寻求撤销裁决的权利，以进一步巩固这一最终结果。这些协议及其有效性在不同的司法管辖区和法律传统中存在很大差异。

National Legislation Permitting Waiver Agreements 国家立法允许豁免协议

In some countries, national arbitration legislations specifically allow for agreements that exclude or limit applications for annulment under certain circumstances. For instance:

在一些国家，国家仲裁立法明确允许在某些情况下排除或限制撤销申请的协议。例如：

  • England : Section 69 of the English Arbitration Act permits parties to exclude court review of arbitral awards, provided they explicitly agree. 英国：《英国仲裁法》第 69 条允许当事人在明确同意的情况下排除法院对仲裁裁决的审查。
  • Belgium : Article 1717(4) of the Belgian Judicial Code allows the exclusion of annulment applications. 比利时：比利时司法法典第 1717(4) 条允许排除撤销申请。
  • Switzerland : Articles 190 and 192 of the Swiss Law on Private International Law support such waivers, enhancing the autonomy of the parties involved. 瑞士：《瑞士国际私法》第 190 条和第 192 条支持此类豁免，增强了有关各方的自主权。

Invalidation of Waiver Agreements 豁免协议无效

Conversely, other jurisdictions do not uphold these agreements, emphasizing the importance of judicial oversight over arbitral awards to ensure fairness and justice:

相反，其他司法管辖区并不支持这些协议，强调司法监督仲裁裁决以确保公平和公正的重要性：

  • France : The French Court d’Appel, in its decision on November 14, 2004 (2005 Rev.arb. 751), invalidated such waivers. 法国：法国上诉法院在 2004 年 11 月 14 日的裁决中（2005 Rev.arb. 751）宣布此类豁免无效。
  • United States : The US Supreme Court, in Hall Street v. Mattel, ruled against agreements that exclude judicial review of arbitral awards. 美国：美国最高法院在霍尔街诉美泰案中驳回了排除对仲裁裁决进行司法审查的协议。

Heightened Judicial Review 加强司法审查

Parties may also agree to subject arbitral awards to heightened judicial review, beyond the typically limited scope:

当事人还可以同意对仲裁裁决进行强化司法审查，超出通常有限的范围：

  • Not Upheld : 不予支持：
    • The U.S. 9th Circuit Court of Appeals, in Kyocera Corp. v. Prudential Bache Trade Serv. , and Aerojet-Gen. Corp v. Am. Arbitration Ass’n , did not uphold such agreements. 美国第九巡回上诉法院，京瓷公司诉 Prudential Bache Trade Serv 案。和Aerojet-Gen。公司诉Am。仲裁协会不支持此类协议。
  • Upheld : 维持：
    • The U.S. 5th Circuit Court of Appeals, in Gateway Tech v. MCI Telecom , upheld the agreement for heightened judicial review. 美国第五巡回上诉法院在Gateway Tech 诉 MCI Telecom 案中维持了加强司法审查的协议。

Consequences of Annulling International Arbitral Awards 撤销国际仲裁裁决的后果

The consequences of annulling an arbitral award as opposed to refusing recognition have significant implications:

与拒绝承认相比，撤销仲裁裁决的后果具有重大影响：

  1. Non-Recognition of the Award : 不承认该裁决：
    1. The award remains legally binding within its issuing jurisdiction but loses its enforceability internationally. 该裁决在其裁决管辖范围内仍然具有法律约束力，但失去了国际可执行性。
  2. Annulment of the Award : 撤销裁决：
    1. The award ceases to exist legally, meaning there is no longer any award to be recognized or enforced. 该裁决不再合法存在，这意味着不再有任何裁决可供承认或执行。

Annulment completely nullifies the legal standing of an award, removing it from the realm of enforceable decisions. This dramatically differs from non-recognition, where the award remains binding in its issuing jurisdiction but cannot be enforced elsewhere.

撤销裁决的法律地位完全无效，将其从可执行决定的范围中删除。这与不承认有很大不同，在不承认的情况下，裁决在其颁发管辖范围内仍然具有约束力，但不能在其他地方执行。

In summary, the global arbitration landscape reveals a mixed approach to agreements waiving the right to seek annulment. Jurisdictions vary from permitting to invalidating such agreements, influencing the finality of arbitral awards and shaping international arbitration practices.

总之，全球仲裁格局揭示了放弃寻求撤销权的协议的混合方法。司法管辖区从允许此类协议到无效此类协议各不相同，影响仲裁裁决的终局性并影响国际仲裁实践。

法院在投资者与国家仲裁中的作用

In investor-state arbitration, the role of national courts varies significantly between non-ICSID cases and those governed by the ICSID Convention. Understanding these differences is crucial when drafting arbitration agreements and selecting dispute resolution forums under investment treaties.

在投资者与国家仲裁中，国家法院的作用在非 ICSID 案件和受 ICSID 公约管辖的案件之间存在显着差异。在起草仲裁协议和选择投资条约下的争议解决论坛时，了解这些差异至关重要。

Comparison: ICSID Convention vs. New York Convention 比较：ICSID 公约与纽约公约：

  1. Scope 范围：
  • The ICSID Convention is designed exclusively for disputes between investors and states, while the New York Convention applies broadly to international arbitration. ICSID 公约专门针对投资者与国家之间的争端，而纽约公约则广泛适用于国际仲裁。
  1. Focus 重点：
  • The ICSID Convention offers a comprehensive legal framework (lex arbitri) that governs the entire arbitration process and the resultant award. In contrast, the New York Convention is predominantly concerned with the post-arbitral process, focusing on the recognition and enforcement of arbitral awards. ICSID 公约提供了一个全面的法律框架（lex arbitri）来管理整个仲裁过程和由此产生的裁决。相比之下，《纽约公约》主要关注仲裁后程序，重点关注仲裁裁决的承认和执行。
  1. Dependence on National Courts 对国家法院的依赖：
  • The ICSID Convention minimizes national court involvement, relying on them only as last-resort enforcers of awards. The New York Convention necessitates national courts to enforce both arbitration agreements and awards, thereby relying on national laws. ICSID 公约最大限度地减少了国家法院的参与，仅依靠它们作为裁决的最后执行者。 《纽约公约》要求国家法院执行仲裁协议和裁决，从而依赖国家法律。
  1. Review Powers 审查权力：
  • Under the ICSID Convention , national courts cannot review ICSID awards. However, the New York Convention permits national courts to refuse the enforcement of awards under specific conditions outlined in Article V. 根据ICSID 公约，国家法院不能审查 ICSID 裁决。然而，《纽约公约》允许国家法院在第五条规定的特定条件下拒绝执行裁决。

Provisions of the Trans-Pacific Partnership (TPP) 跨太平洋伙伴关系协定（TPP）的规定

Article 4, Chapter 9 of the TPP outlines various arbitration options for claimants, including the ICSID Convention, ICSID Additional Facility Rules, UNCITRAL Arbitration Rules, or any mutually agreed arbitral institution or rules.

TPP第9章第4条概述了申请人的各种仲裁选择，包括ICSID公约、ICSID附加便利规则、UNCITRAL仲裁规则或任何共同商定的仲裁机构或规则。

ICSID’s “Self-Contained” System ICSID 的“独立”系统

  1. Exclusivity (Article 26) : Once parties consent to ICSID arbitration, it becomes the sole remedy. 排他性（第26条） ：一旦当事人同意ICSID仲裁，它就成为唯一的补救措施。
  2. Diplomatic Protection (Article 27) : Member states cannot provide diplomatic protection, except in limited circumstances. 外交保护（第27条） ：除有限情况外，成员国不能提供外交保护。
  3. Immunity (Articles 21 and 22) : Participants in ICSID arbitration enjoy immunity from legal processes. 豁免权（第 21 条和第 22 条） ：ICSID 仲裁参与者享有法律程序豁免权。
  4. Post-Award Remedies (Articles 49 to 52) : Remedies are limited to supplementation or rectification, interpretation, revision, and annulment as defined by the Convention. 裁决后补救措施（第 49 条至第 52 条） ：补救措施仅限于《公约》规定的补充或纠正、解释、修订和废止。
  5. Finality (Article 53) : ICSID awards are final and binding, and courts of member states cannot annul them. 最终性（第 53 条） ：ICSID 裁决是最终裁决并具有约束力，成员国法院不能撤销裁决。
  6. Enforcement (Article 54) : All member states are obligated to recognize and enforce the monetary parts of ICSID awards. 执行（第 54 条） ：所有成员国都有义务承认和执行 ICSID 裁决的货币部分。
  7. Place of Proceedings (Articles 62 and 63) : The location of arbitration hearings does not affect the legal significance of the proceedings. 诉讼地点（第 62 条和第 63 条） ：仲裁审理地点不影响诉讼程序的法律意义。

In conclusion, while both the ICSID and New York Conventions play vital roles in supporting the investor-state arbitration system, their differences in scope, focus, reliance on national courts, and review powers illustrate the varying degrees of national court involvement. The ICSID Convention’s self-contained nature underscores its autonomy from national legal systems, ensuring a more predictable and uniform arbitration process.

总之，虽然《投资争端解决中心》和《纽约公约》在支持投资者与国家仲裁制度方面发挥着至关重要的作用，但它们在范围、重点、对国家法院的依赖和审查权方面的差异说明了国家法院参与程度的不同。 ICSID 公约的独立性强调其独立于国家法律体系，确保仲裁程序更加可预测和统一。

国家法院的作用——《纽约公约》下的执行职能

In the realm of international arbitration, the interplay between the arbitral process and national courts is indispensable. Neil Kaplan aptly highlights this necessity by contrasting the unrealistic ideal of a perfect arbitration world with the pragmatic realities of arbitration practice. In practice, the national courts’ enforcement function is crucial to ensure the efficacy and finality of arbitral awards.

在国际仲裁领域，仲裁程序与各国法院之间的相互作用是不可或缺的。尼尔·卡普兰通过将完美仲裁世界的不切实际理想与仲裁实践的务实现实进行对比，恰当地强调了这种必要性。在实践中，各国法院的执行职能对于确保仲裁裁决的有效性和终局性至关重要。

Enforcement Role under the New York Convention (NYC)

The New York Convention (NYC) is a cornerstone of international arbitration, with 156 state parties committed to recognizing and enforcing arbitral awards. Under Articles II and III of the NYC, contracting states must treat non-domestic awards similarly to domestic awards, ensuring their enforceability.

《纽约公约》(NYC) 是国际仲裁的基石，有 156 个缔约国承诺承认和执行仲裁裁决。根据《纽约公约》第二条和第三条，缔约国必须以与国内裁决类似的方式对待非国内裁决，以确保其可执行性。

Court Obligations 法院义务

National courts under the NYC have two primary obligations:

纽约市下属的国家法院有两项主要义务：

  1. Uphold and enforce arbitration agreements. 维护并执行仲裁协议。
  2. Deny parties court access in contravention of their arbitration agreement, promoting the arbitration process and respecting parties’ intentions. 拒绝当事人违反仲裁协议进入法院，促进仲裁进程并尊重当事人的意愿。

Grounds for Refusal of Enforcement 拒绝执行的理由

Article V of the NYC sets out specific grounds upon which courts can refuse to enforce an arbitral award:

《纽约公约》第五条规定了法院拒绝执行仲裁裁决的具体理由：

  1. Incapacity or Invalidity : The parties to the arbitration agreement lacked capacity, or the agreement was not valid under governing law. 无行为能力或无效：仲裁协议当事人无行为能力，或协议根据适用法律无效。
  2. Procedural Fairness : The party against whom the award is invoked was not given proper notice or was unable to present their case adequately. 程序公平性：裁决所针对的一方没有得到适当的通知或无法充分陈述其案件。
  3. Scope of Arbitration : The award contains decisions beyond what was submitted to arbitration. 仲裁范围：裁决包含超出提交仲裁范围的决定。
  4. Arbitration Procedure : The procedure or composition of the arbitral tribunal was not in accordance with the parties’ agreement or local law. 仲裁程序：仲裁庭的程序或组成不符合当事人的协议或当地法律。
  5. Binding Nature : The award is not yet binding or has been set aside/suspended in its country of origin. 约束性质：该裁决尚未具有约束力或已在其原籍国被搁置/暂停。
  6. Arbitrability : The subject matter is not capable of settlement by arbitration under local law. 可仲裁性：根据当地法律，标的事项不能通过仲裁解决。
  7. Public Policy : Enforcement would be contrary to the public policy of the enforcement state. 公共政策：执行将违反执行国的公共政策。

Recognition Across Jurisdictions 跨司法管辖区的认可

In theory, awards rendered in one signatory state should be enforceable in any other signatory state, except under the exceptional circumstances delineated in Article V. National courts, therefore, play an exclusive role in processing and enforcing these awards, emphasizing the need for judicial support in the international arbitration framework.

理论上，除第五条规定的特殊情况外，一个签署国作出的裁决应在任何其他签署国可执行。因此，国家法院在处理和执行这些裁决方面发挥着排他性作用，强调司法支持的必要性在国际仲裁框架内。

ICSID Annulment vs. NYC Set-Aside ICSID 撤销与纽约公约撤销

While the NYC focuses on enforcement, ICSID (International Centre for Settlement of Investment Disputes) and UNCITRAL (United Nations Commission on International Trade Law) systems also address annulment:

虽然纽约市侧重于执行，但 ICSID（国际投资争端解决中心）和 UNCITRAL（联合国国际贸易法委员会）系统也处理撤销问题：

  • ICSID System : Annulment follows a structured process within the ICSID framework. ICSID 系统：撤销遵循 ICSID 框架内的结构化流程。
  • UNCITRAL System : Annulment is governed by national law, specifically the law of the arbitration seat. Only the courts at the seat of arbitration are competent to annul the award, following grounds specified in Article 34 of the UNCITRAL Model Law. 联合国国际贸易法委员会制度：撤销受国家法律管辖，特别是仲裁地的法律。只有仲裁地法院有权根据《贸易法委员会示范法》第 34 条规定的理由撤销裁决。

In conclusion, the national courts’ role in enforcing arbitral awards under the New York Convention is pivotal. Their involvement ensures adherence to international arbitration agreements and awards, maintaining the integrity and consistency of the arbitration process globally. Courts must balance their national interests with international obligations, fostering a cooperative international arbitration environment.

总之，各国法院在执行《纽约公约》下的仲裁裁决方面的作用至关重要。他们的参与确保了国际仲裁协议和裁决的遵守，维护全球仲裁程序的完整性和一致性。法院必须平衡国家利益与国际义务，营造合作的国际仲裁环境。

附录：期末重点

Consent

In the context of international arbitration, “consent” refers to the mutual agreement between parties to submit their disputes to arbitration rather than resolving them through litigation in national courts. This consent is considered the cornerstone of arbitration because it serves as the fundamental basis for the arbitrator’s authority to resolve disputes. The arbitration agreement, where the parties explicitly express this consent, is crucial for the initiation and legitimacy of the arbitration process.

Over time, the concept of consent in arbitration has evolved due to the complexities introduced by multiparty disputes, investment arbitration, and other modern developments. While traditionally, arbitration was purely consensual and based on direct agreements, today’s consent can also be derived through various forms such as national investment laws, bilateral and multilateral treaties, and asymmetrical agreements where one party initiates arbitration unilaterally. Despite these developments, the foundational principle that arbitration rests on the parties’ agreement remains critical.

在国际仲裁的背景下，“同意”是指双方同意将争议提交仲裁解决，而不是通过国家法院诉讼解决。这种同意被认为是仲裁的基石，因为它是仲裁员解决争议的根本依据。通过仲裁协议，双方明确表达这种同意，这对仲裁程序的启动和合法性至关重要。

随着时间的推移，由于多方争议、投资仲裁和其他现代发展的复杂性，仲裁中的同意概念已经演变。虽然传统上仲裁是纯粹自愿且基于直接协议的，但今天的同意也可以通过各种形式获得，如国家投资法、双边和多边条约以及一方单方面启动仲裁的不对称协议等形式。尽管这些发展存在，仲裁以当事人协议为基础的基本原则仍然是至关重要的。

It is important to note that there is a difference between the consent to an arbitration agreement (for example, through oral communication) and the formal validity of the arbitration agreement (which may require writing or signatures). In most cases, consent to the arbitration clause is often confirmed by the parties reaching an agreement on the main or underlying contract that contains the arbitration clause. Regardless of the principle of the independence of arbitration clauses, a party’s commitment to the underlying contract often implies acceptance of the arbitration clause contained within it. However, disputes may arise in the following situations:

  1. A party acknowledges the main or underlying contract but does not acknowledge the arbitration clause (for example, they are unaware of such a clause or have impliedly rejected it); or
  2. The underlying contract is not established, but the parties have separately reached an agreement on the arbitration clause (for example, they agreed on a dispute resolution method during contract negotiations).

In these cases, courts and arbitral tribunals will separately determine whether the parties have agreed to the independent arbitration clause, regardless of whether they have agreed to the underlying contract.

If a party initiates arbitration proceedings or participates in arbitration proceedings without raising objections, it can be considered as effective consent to the arbitration agreement. Article 16(2) of the UNCITRAL Model Law requires that objections to arbitral jurisdiction should not be raised after the submission of a statement of defense; otherwise, jurisdictional objections will be precluded. Similar provisions exist in other domestic laws.

From a practical perspective, situations where jurisdictional objections are waived occur frequently, thus laying the foundation for the validity of subsequent arbitration proceedings and arbitral awards.

需要注意的是，存在仲裁协议的合意（例如通过口头沟通）和仲裁协议的形式合法性（可能需要书面或签字）之间是有区别的。在大多数情况下，仲裁条款的合意通常通过当事人对包含仲裁条款的主合同或基础合同达成一致来确认。不论仲裁条款独立性的原则，一方当事人对基础合同的承诺往往意味着其对包含在该合同中的仲裁条款的接受。但是，在以下情形下可能会发生争议：

  1. 一方认可主合同或基础合同，但不认可仲裁条款（例如，不知道该条款的存在或暗示不接受此条款）；或
  2. 基础合同未成立，但当事人单独就仲裁条款达成了一致（例如，在缔约谈判过程中同意争议解决方式）。

在这些情况下，法院和仲裁庭会单独判断当事人是否就独立的仲裁条款达成一致，而不考虑是否已就基础合同达成一致。

一方当事人启动仲裁程序或参与仲裁程序而未提出异议，可以作为其有效同意仲裁协议的依据。《联合国国际贸易法委员会示范法》第16条第2款要求，在提交答辩状后不得提出对仲裁庭管辖权的抗辩，否则将不予受理。其他国内法也有类似规定。

从实践角度来看，放弃管辖权异议的情形经常发生，从而为后续的仲裁程序及仲裁裁决的有效性奠定基础。

From the perspective of drafting agreements, this means that the arbitration agreement should (and typically does) explicitly state that disputes are to be resolved through “arbitration”—not through expert determination, mediation, “alternative dispute resolution,” or some other form of dispute resolution. Under many international treaties and arbitration legislation, these other forms of alternative dispute resolution are not considered “arbitration” and do not benefit from the pro-enforcement bias provided by these laws. Thus, the commitment by the parties that “all disputes shall be finally resolved by arbitration” is a crucial element of any international arbitration agreement.

Similarly, most arbitration agreements stipulate that disputes should be submitted to arbitration, where the arbitral tribunal will issue a “binding” or “final” award (rather than a consultative recommendation). Moreover, arbitration clauses should treat arbitration as mandatory, not as one of several options available to the parties in case of future disputes. Therefore, arbitration clauses typically (and should) stipulate that “all disputes shall be finally resolved by arbitration…”

从协议起草的角度来看，这意味着仲裁协议应当（并且通常）明确规定将争议提交“仲裁”解决，而非提交专家认定、调解、“替代性争议解决方式”或其他一些争议解决方式。在许多国际条约及仲裁立法下，这些其他形式的替代性争议解决方式不会被视为“仲裁”，并且不会享有这些法律下所提供的“倾向于强制执行”的保护。因此，当事人承诺“全部争议应当交由仲裁作终局性解决……”是任何国际仲裁协议的关键要素。

类似地，大多数仲裁协议约定争议应当提交仲裁，由仲裁庭作出“有约束力的”或“终局”的裁决（而非咨询性建议）。此外，仲裁条款应当将仲裁视为强制性的，而非当事人未来发生争议时可选择的争议解决方式之一。因此，仲裁条款通常（也应当）约定“全部争议应当交由仲裁作终局性解决……”

  1. 仲裁协议

Arbitration agreements are largely the product of the interests, negotiations, and drafting skills of the parties involved. Article 7(1) of the UNCITRAL Model Law provides that an arbitration agreement can take the form of an arbitration clause in a contract or a separate agreement. Based on the freedom granted by this provision, parties can incorporate their arbitration agreement into the main commercial contract or draft a separate “arbitration agreement.” The arbitration clauses can vary in length and form. Domestic courts also recognize very brief arbitration clauses, such as “English law — arbitration, if required, under ICC rules, London” or “Arbitration - Hamburg, Germany.” Another extreme example is that in large transactions, arbitration agreements sometimes appear as documents that need to be separately signed, stretching over dozens of pages and (reportedly) covering every possible procedural issue. Arbitration agreements provide a mechanism for resolving future disputes that have not yet occurred (and ideally, may never happen).

International arbitration agreements typically include the following elements: (1) agreement to arbitrate; (2) scope of disputes to be submitted to arbitration; (3) applicable arbitration institution and its rules; (4) seat of arbitration; (5) the method for appointing arbitrators, including their number and qualifications; (6) language of arbitration; and (7) choice of law clause.

仲裁协议很大程度上是当事人利益、协商和起草技巧的产物。《联合国国际贸易法委员会示范法》第7条第1款规定，仲裁协议可以采取合同中仲裁条款的形式或单独的协议形式。基于该条款所赋予的自由权，当事人在起草仲裁协议时可以将其载入实体商业合同中，也可以起草独立的“仲裁协议”，仲裁条款也可以写成长短不一的任何形式。国内法院同样认可非常简短的仲裁条款，如“英格兰法——（如需）仲裁，依据国际商会规则，伦敦”或“仲裁——汉堡，德国”。另一种极端情形是，大型交易中的仲裁协议有时会以需要单独签署的文件的形式出现，长达几十页并且（据称）约定了每一项可能发生的程序事宜。仲裁协议提供的是尚未发生的（可能的话，希望永远不会发生的）未来争议的解决机制。

国际仲裁协议通常包括以下要素：（1）仲裁的合意；（2）提交仲裁的争议范围；（3）仲裁机构及其规则的适用；（4）仲裁地；（5）指定仲裁员的方法及仲裁员的人数、资质;（6）仲裁语言；以及（7）法律选择条款。

  1. Enforceability

The New York Convention on the Recognition and Enforcement of Foreign Arbitral Awards of 1958, obliges signatory States to not only recognize and enforce arbitral awards but also valid arbitration agreements. This fundamental principle of arbitration law, in combination with the separability of arbitration agreements and the competence-competence doctrine, all provide arbitration agreements with robust protection. That said, the validity of the arbitration agreement itself is a threshold consideration in determining its recognition and enforceability.

1958 年《承认和执行外国仲裁裁决纽约公约》规定签署国不仅有义务承认和执行仲裁裁决，而且有义务承认和执行有效的仲裁协议。仲裁法的这一基本原则，结合仲裁协议的可分离性和能力-能力原则，都为仲裁协议提供了强有力的保护。也就是说，仲裁协议本身的有效性是决定其承认和执行的门槛。

  1. 香港的执行

The courts in the Hong Kong Special Administrative Region (SAR) are pro-enforcement of arbitral awards. The applicable domestic legal framework for enforcing arbitral awards in Hong Kong SAR is set out in the Arbitration Ordinance (Cap 609).

Under the domestic legal framework, Hong Kong SAR courts have continually demonstrated their support for arbitration and emphasized in judgments that they will only interfere in limited circumstances. The pro-arbitration approach of the Hong Kong SAR courts has underpinned Hong Kong SAR’s position as a popular destination for dispute resolution and will give companies comfort that arbitral awards in their favor can be enforced in Hong Kong SAR.

Awards in jurisdictions that are parties to the New York Convention need to be enforced using a two-stage process. Given the pro-arbitration approach adopted by the Hong Kong SAR courts, the award will be recognized unless one of the grounds provided under the Arbitration Ordinance applies.

Meanwhile, the process to enforce awards made in mainland China and the Macao SAR is generally more straightforward given the special arrangements that exist with the Hong Kong SAR and can usually be enforced without difficulty. When companies are negotiating the dispute resolution clause in their contracts, they should consider the benefits of Hong Kong SAR in terms of it being a recognized forum to resolve disputes and also the ability to enforce (with ease) against a party in mainland China or Macao SAR.

香港特别行政区的法院对仲裁裁决采取支持执行的态度。香港特别行政区的仲裁裁决执行适用的国内法律框架由《仲裁条例》（第609章）规定。

在该国内法律框架下，香港特别行政区的法院一直展示出对仲裁的支持，并在判决中强调他们只会在有限的情况下进行干预。香港特别行政区法院的亲仲裁态度巩固了香港特别行政区作为争议解决热门地位，这将使公司确信他们有利的仲裁裁决可以在香港特别行政区执行。

在作为《纽约公约》缔约方的司法管辖区内作出的裁决需要通过两阶段程序执行。鉴于香港特别行政区法院所采纳的亲仲裁态度，除非适用《仲裁条例》规定的某一拒绝执行的理由，该裁决将被认定。

同时，由于与香港特别行政区的特别安排，在中国大陆和澳门特别行政区作出的裁决一般更为简单且无困难地执行。当公司在其合同中谈判争议解决条款时，他们应考虑香港特别行政区作为公认的争议解决论坛及易于对中国大陆或澳门特别行政区方强制执行的优势。

Enforceable Arbitral Awards in Hong Kong SAR 在香港特别行政区可执行的仲裁裁决

Once the court has granted permission to enforce an arbitral award, it may be enforced in the same manner as a court judgment regardless of whether it was made in or outside of Hong Kong SAR.

The award should be in writing and be signed by the arbitral tribunal. If the award has not yet become binding on the parties or has been set aside or suspended by a competent authority, the award cannot be enforced.

An award must result from an agreement to arbitrate and must represent the final decision of the arbitral tribunal on a substantive issue. An award includes an interim award and an award on the costs of the arbitration. However, a decision resolving a procedural issue is generally not considered an award.

Arbitral awards that can be enforced in Hong Kong SAR include Convention awards, mainland awards, Macao SAR awards, and other awards which include awards made in Hong Kong SAR:

  • A Convention award means an arbitral award made in a state or the territory of a state which is a party to the Convention on the Recognition and Enforcement of Foreign Awards, also known as the New York Convention. This does not include the People’s Republic of China (PRC) or any part of the PRC.
  • For mainland and Macao SAR awards, arbitral awards made in mainland China by a recognized mainland arbitral authority in accordance with the Arbitration Law of the PRC or made in Macao SAR are enforceable in Hong Kong SAR pursuant to special arrangements in place.

一旦法院允许执行仲裁裁决，该裁决可被如同法院判决一样执行，无论其是本地还是国外作出的。

裁决应为书面的，并由仲裁庭签署。如果裁决尚未对双方有约束力或已被有权机关撤销或中止，则该裁决无法执行。

裁决须基于仲裁协议并代表仲裁庭对实质问题的最终决定。裁决包括临时裁决和仲裁费用的裁决。然而，解决程序性问题的决定通常不被视为裁决。

在香港特别行政区可执行的仲裁裁决包括《纽约公约》裁决、内地裁决、澳门特别行政区裁决及其他裁决（包括香港特别行政区作出的裁决）：

  • 《纽约公约》裁决指在缔约国或缔约国领土内作出的仲裁裁决，亦称为《承认与执行外国仲裁裁决公约》。这不包括中华人民共和国（中国大陆）或其任何部分。
  • 对于内地和澳门特别行政区裁决，由中国大陆认定的仲裁机构根据《中华人民共和国仲裁法》作出的仲裁裁决或在澳门特别行政区作出的裁决，根据特定的安排在香港特别行政区可执行。

Enforcement of an Arbitral Award in Hong Kong SAR 在香港特别行政区执行仲裁裁决

There are two stages in the enforcement of an arbitral award in Hong Kong SAR:

  1. Recognition Stage – An award is converted into a Hong Kong SAR judgment.
  2. Execution Stage – The judgment can be enforced using an acceptable method of enforcement.

At the recognition stage, the court has to decide whether to grant permission to enforce the award. An application to the High Court for leave to enforce an award may be made ex-parte by affidavit. The applicant must make full and frank disclosure of relevant information to the court in support of the application. If the award is in order and the court grants permission, it will give judgment “in terms of” the award. A party may then enforce the arbitral award by pursuing the same enforcement methods for court judgments, such as statutory demand, charging order, or writ of execution.

在香港特别行政区执行仲裁裁决有两个阶段：

  1. 认可阶段 – 将裁决转换为香港特别行政区法院判决；
  2. 执行阶段 – 使用认可的执行方法执行判决。

在认可阶段，法院决定是否授予执行裁决的许可。可通过宣誓书向高等法院申请准许执行裁决。申请人必须向法院提供全部及坦率的相关信息披露以支持申请。如果裁决无误且法院授予许可，将给予“依裁决内容”的判决。此后，一方可以通过法院判决的相同执行方法来执行仲裁裁决，如法定偿还令、扣押令或执行令。

Refusal of Enforcement of an Arbitral Award

The grounds for the court to refuse to enforce an arbitral award are almost identical for all categories of awards. They are exclusively procedural as there is no right to appeal an award on a question of law.

For Convention awards, mainland awards and Macao SAR awards, the reasons are exhaustive. The court cannot refuse to enforce these awards for other reasons.

The court may refuse to enforce these awards if:

  • a party to the arbitration agreement was under some incapacity;
  • the arbitration agreement was not valid under the law applicable to the contract;
  • the person was not given proper notice of the appointment of the arbitrator or of the arbitral proceedings or was unable to present their case;
  • the award deals with a difference not contemplated by or not falling within the terms of submission to arbitration or contains decisions on matters beyond the scope of the submission to arbitration;
  • the composition of the arbitral authority or the arbitral procedure was not in accordance with the agreement of the parties; or
  • the award has not yet become binding on the parties or has been set aside or suspended by a competent authority.

The court may also refuse to enforce an award if the subject matter of the award is not capable of settlement by arbitration under the law of Hong Kong SAR; or if it would be contrary to public policy to enforce the award.

If an award is not a Convention award, a mainland award, or a Macao SAR award, the court can refuse to enforce an award if the applicant can prove one of the grounds for refusal of enforcement as discussed above. Additionally, the court in this case has the discretion to refuse to enforce an arbitral award for any other reason if the court considers it “just to do so”.

法院拒绝执行仲裁裁决的理由对所有类别的裁决几乎是相同的。它们仅限于程序性事项，因为没有法律问题上上诉裁决的权利。

对于《纽约公约》裁决、内地裁决和澳门特别行政区裁决，这些理由是详尽无遗的。法院不能以其他理由拒绝执行这些裁决。

法院可以拒绝执行这些裁决的情况包括：

  • 仲裁协议当事方有某种无行为能力；
  • 仲裁协议在适用合同的法律下无效；
  • 未及时通知当事方仲裁员的任命或仲裁程序，或当事方无法陈述其案件；
  • 裁决处理的争议不在仲裁提交的术语内或包含超出仲裁提交范畴的决定；
  • 仲裁机构的组成或仲裁程序不符合当事人的协议；或
  • 裁决尚未对当事方有约束力或已被有权机关撤销或中止。

法院也可以拒绝执行裁决如果裁决的标的事项在香港特别行政区法律下不能通过仲裁解决；如果执行裁决会违反公共政策。

如果裁决不是《纽约公约》裁决、内地裁决或澳门特别行政区裁决，法院可以如上讨论的理由由申请人证明后拒绝执行裁决。在这种情况下，法院也有自由裁量权在认为“公正”的情况下拒绝执行仲裁裁决。

Cost to Enforce an Arbitral Award 执行仲裁裁决的成本

An enforcing party generally pays for its own costs of the enforcement application, unless otherwise ordered by the court. When enforcement is unsuccessfully challenged, the court will normally award costs against the challenging party on an indemnity basis, which means the recovery rate will be higher than on a standard basis.

除非法院另有规定，执行方通常支付其执行申请的费用。当执行受到挑战且失败时，法院通常会依据赔偿性方式对挑战方判处费用，这意味着恢复率会高于标准方式。

Arbitrability

Arbitration is a private dispute resolution process in which parties agree to refer disputes to a tribunal and accept the outcome, rather than using a national court. It is grounded in the freedom of parties to contract, and so only matters which parties can make subject to a private contract can be referred to arbitration.

仲裁是一种私人争议解决程序，当事人同意将争议提交给仲裁庭并接受其裁决，而不是使用国家法院。它基于当事人的合同自由，因此只有当事人可以通过私人合同解决的事项才能提交仲裁。

This principle is reflected in several key international treaties and laws. For example, Article II (1) of the New York Convention (1958) provides that “Each Contracting State shall recognize an agreement in writing under which the parties undertake to submit to arbitration all or any differences which have arisen or which may arise between them in respect of a defined legal relationship, whether contractual or not, concerning a subject matter capable of settlement by arbitration.”

Articles 34(2)(b)(i) and 36(1)(b)(i) of the UNCITRAL Model Law (with amendments as adopted in 2006) provide that an arbitral award can be set aside if “… the court finds that… the subject matter of the dispute is not capable of settlement by arbitration under the laws of this State…” and “Recognition or enforcement of an arbitral award, irrespective of the country in which it was made, may be refused only… if the court finds that… the subject matter of the dispute is not capable of settlement by arbitration under the law of this State…”

这一点在几项关键的国际条约和法律中得到体现。例如，1958年《纽约公约》第二条第一款规定：“每一缔约国应承认当事人书面协议约定将他们之间已经发生或可能发生的所有或任何争议提交仲裁解决，前提是这些争议涉及特定法律关系，不论为契约性质与否。”1985年《联合国国际贸易法委员会国际商事仲裁示范法》（2006年修订）第34(2)(b)(i)条和第36(1)(b)(i)条规定，如果“……法院认定……争议标的物根据该国法律不能通过仲裁解决……”，仲裁裁决可以被撤销，而“无论该裁决在哪个国家作出”，如果“法院认定……争议标的物根据该国法律不能通过仲裁解决……”可以拒绝承认或执行。

However, the categories of what are and what are not arbitrable vary from jurisdiction to jurisdiction although there are a number of well-recognized categories of dispute that may not be capable of being resolved by arbitration. A dispute will generally not be arbitrable if it involves an issue of public policy, public rights or the interests of third parties, or where the dispute in question is clearly covered by a statutory provision that provides for unassailable access to a nation’s judicial or other official public systems of dispute resolution.

但是，可仲裁事项的类别因司法管辖区而异，尽管有许多公认的争议类别不能通过仲裁解决。如果争议涉及公共政策、公共权利或第三方利益，或争议显然被法律规定提供不可动摇的国家司法或其他官方公共争议解决的主旨。” 1985年《联合国国际贸易法委员会国际商事仲裁示范法》（2006年修订）第34(2)(b)(i)条和第36(1)(b)(i)条规定，如果“……法院认定……争议标的物根据该国法律不能通过仲裁解决……”，仲裁裁决可以被撤销，而“无论该裁决在哪个国家作出”，如果“法院认定……争议标的物根据该国法律不能通过仲裁解决……”，仲裁裁决的承认或执行可以被拒绝。

Countries have different stipulations regarding what matters are considered non-arbitrable. Generally, disputes or claims that are deemed “non-arbitrable” usually have significant public importance or require judicial protection due to recognized needs. Many countries do not allow arbitration for disputes involving criminal law, labor disputes, intellectual property, real estate, bankruptcy, or family and marriage matters.

各国对于哪些事项属于不可仲裁事项有不同的规定。一般而言，被认为“不可仲裁”的争议或主张通常具有重大公共意义或需要司法保护的公认需求。许多国家不允许将涉及刑法、劳动纠纷、知识产权、房地产、破产或婚姻家庭等争议诉诸仲裁。

Falcon Insurance Co (Hong Kong) Ltd v Bing Lee Crane-Lorry Transportation Co Ltd & Anor [2023] HKCFI 1129 (MP)

A dispute arose in respect of proceedings initiated by an insurer (the plaintiff) seeking a declaration of non-liability. The insurance policy in question was subject to an arbitration clause and the defendant applied for a stay of the proceedings in favour of arbitration. The plaintiff argued that given the claim was for a declaration under the relevant statute, it was non arbitrable and thus no stay should be granted.

因保险公司（原告）提起的寻求无责任声明的诉讼而产生争议。涉案保险单受仲裁条款约束，被告申请中止诉讼以利于仲裁。原告辩称，鉴于该主张是根据相关法规提出的声明，因此不可仲裁，因此不应批准中止。

The Hong Kong Court of First Instance granted an order for stay in favour of arbitration and applied the following principles:-

香港原讼法庭作出有利于仲裁的中止令，并适用以下原则：-

  1. The fact that arbitral tribunal may not have powers to grant certain relief exclusively reserved to the courts does not make the subject matter non arbitrable. 仲裁庭可能无权授予法院专有的某些救济，这一事实并不意味着该主题不可仲裁。
  2. If there is a prima facie or plainly arguable case that the parties are bound by an arbitration agreement, the matter should be stayed for the arbitral tribunal to determine its own jurisdiction. 如果有表面证据或明显有争议的情况表明当事人受仲裁协议的约束，则该事项应留待仲裁庭确定其管辖权。
  3. The perceived lack of merits of any defence does not mean there is no genuine dispute that should be referred to the contractually agreed resolution forum (i.e., arbitration). 认为任何抗辩缺乏优点并不意味着不存在应提交合同约定的解决论坛（即仲裁）的真正争议。

Grandom Asia Holding Ltd v. Henry Wai & Co (A Firm) [2018] HKCFI 31; HCMP 1700/2017 (10 January 2018)

In a decision dated 10 January 2018, the Hong Kong Court of First Instance (Court) stayed its proceedings in favour of arbitration under an arbitration agreement between a firm of solicitors and its former clients. The Court held that there is nothing in Hong Kong law or public policy to indicate that a dispute between a solicitor’s firm and its client over fees is not arbitrable. Hong Kong law protects consumers from being forced into arbitration, but the law will consider the nature of the transaction to determine whether or not a claimant is truly acting as a consumer. 香港原讼法庭于 2018 年 1 月 10日作出裁决，中止诉讼程序，转而根据一家律师事务所与其前客户之间达成的仲裁协议进行仲裁。法院认为，香港法律或公共政策中没有任何内容表明律师事务所与其客户之间的费用纠纷不可仲裁。香港法律保护消费者免遭强制仲裁，但法律会考虑交易的性质来确定索赔人是否真正充当消费者。

The Court was asked to decide whether the Arbitration Agreement was enforceable, and whether the Court’s proceedings should be stayed in favour of arbitration.

法院被要求决定仲裁协议是否可执行，以及法院的诉讼程序是否应中止以利于仲裁。

The decision of the Court establishes that a dispute between a solicitor and its client is prima facie, arbitrable, and no provisions of Hong Kong law or public policy suggest otherwise. This decision will be welcomed by law firms, including international firms, which frequently include arbitration agreements in their retainers with clients. 法院的裁决确定律师与其委托人之间的纠纷表面上是可仲裁的，并且香港法律或公共政策的规定没有表明其他情况。这一决定将受到包括国际律师事务所在内的律师事务所的欢迎，这些律师事务所经常在与客户的保留中包含仲裁协议。

Moreover, while Hong Kong law protects consumers from being forced into arbitration, the protection is available only to genuine consumers. The courts will look critically at the nature of a dispute (and the underlying transaction), to determine whether a claimant is a consumer under Section 4 (1) of CECO. No party should be allowed to take advantage of statutory protections to avoid an agreement to arbitrate to which it has previously consented.

此外，虽然香港法律保护消费者不被迫接受仲裁，但这种保护只适用于真正的消费者。法院将严格审查争议的性质（以及相关交易），以确定索赔人是否是《CECO》第 4 (1) 条规定的消费者。任何一方均不得利用法定保护来避免达成其先前同意的仲裁协议。

Once again, the Hong Kong Court has reiterated that a party challenging the validity of an arbitration agreement must approach the courts only in exceptional situations. If parties take the risk of challenging an arbitration agreement, they must be prepared to bear the financial brunt, including payment of indemnity costs if their challenge fails.

香港法院再次重申，质疑仲裁协议有效性的一方只有在特殊情况下才必须向法院提起诉讼。如果当事人冒着质疑仲裁协议的风险，他们必须做好承受财务冲击的准备，包括在质疑失败时支付赔偿费用。

Competence-Competence

Kompetenz-kompetenz, or compétence-compétence, is a jurisprudential doctrine whereby a legal body, such as a arbitral tribunal, may have competence, or jurisdiction, to rule as to the extent of its own competence on an issue before it. This doctrine is reflected in Article 16 of the UNCITRAL Model Law on International Commercial Arbitration (“Model Law”) and incorporated in section 34 of the Arbitration Ordinance (Cap. 341) (“Ordinance”). Kompetenz-kompetenz，或称职权-职权，是一种法理学原则，根据该学说，仲裁庭等法律机构可能拥有能力或管辖权，就其处理的问题对其自身的权限范围做出裁决。这一原则反映在《贸易法委员会国际商事仲裁示范法》（“示范法”）第 16 条中，并纳入《仲裁条例》（第 341 章）（“条例”）第 34 条。

Competence-competence picks up where separability ends. The doctrine has two aspects. Firstly, it means that arbitrators are judges of their own jurisdiction and have the right to rule on their own competence. Therefore, if the validity of the arbitration agreement itself and thus the competence of the arbitrator is impugned, he or she does not have to stop proceedings but can continue the arbitration and consider whether he or she has jurisdiction. Secondly, in some countries, the arbitration agreement ousts the initial jurisdiction of ordinary courts. If the prima facie existence of the arbitration agreement is objected to, a court must refer the dispute to arbitration. But there is great variation where this second aspect is concerned. In civil law countries such as France, arbitrators appear to have wide jurisdiction to determine their competence. The prevalent view in common law countries is that arbitrators have only limited competence to rule on their jurisdiction, and that these rulings may be reopened and scrutinized by the courts.

管辖权优先原则在分离原则终结的地方开始发挥作用。该原则有两个方面。首先，它表示仲裁员是其自身管辖权的裁判者，有权裁定其管辖权。因此，如果仲裁协议本身的有效性及仲裁员的管辖权受到质疑，他或她不必中止程序，而可以继续仲裁并考虑其是否具有管辖权。其次，在一些国家，仲裁协议排除了普通法院的初始管辖权。如果对仲裁协议的表面存在性提出异议，法院必须将争议提交仲裁。然而，对于这一第二方面存在很大差异。在法国等大陆法系国家，仲裁员似乎具有广泛的管辖权来确定其管辖权。普通法国家普遍认为，仲裁员只有有限的管辖权来裁定其管辖权，这些裁定可能会被法院重新审查和审查。

AAA v DDD [2024] HKCFI 513

A Hong Kong court has set aside a tribunal’s finding on jurisdiction, holding that the arbitration clause in a loan agreement did not provide the tribunal with the jurisdiction to determine disputes arising out of a related promissory note that contained its own but different arbitration agreement.

香港一家法院驳回了仲裁庭关于管辖权的裁决，认为贷款协议中的仲裁条款并未赋予仲裁庭裁决因包含其自己但不同仲裁协议的相关本票而引起的争议的管辖权。

In AAA v DDD [2024] HKCFI 513, Deputy High Court Judge Reyes SC considered the situation where there is a set of related contracts and two or more of the contracts have different dispute resolution clauses. The issue was whether the arbitration clause in a loan agreement (and a later amendment agreement) conferred jurisdiction on the tribunal formed under it, to determine related disputes arising out of a promissory note which contained its own arbitration agreement.

在AAA v DDD [2024]HKCFI513 案中，高等法院副法官 Reyes SC 考虑了存在一组相关合同且其中两个或多个合同具有不同争议解决条款的情况。问题是贷款协议（以及后来的修订协议）中的仲裁条款是否赋予根据其组成的仲裁庭管辖权，以裁决因包含其仲裁协议的本票而引起的相关争议。

Under the principle of competence-competence, an arbitral tribunal has the competence to rule on whether it has jurisdiction (competence) to hear a dispute. As Reyes DHCJ observed, an arbitral tribunal’s decision on jurisdiction is not final and may be challenged de novo by an aggrieved party within 30 days from the date of notice of the ruling under section 34(1) of the Arbitration Ordinance, which incorporates Article 16(3) of the UNCITRAL Model Law.

根据管辖权-管辖权原则，仲裁庭有权裁定其是否具有审理争议的管辖权。正如 Reyes DHCJ 所指出的，仲裁庭关于管辖权的决定不是最终的，受害方可以根据《仲裁条例》第 34(1) 条（其中包含第 16 条）在裁决通知之日起 30 天内对管辖权提出重新质疑《贸易法委员会示范法》(3)。

Ryes J said he doubted “that the mere reference to a document and the exhibition of the same to a request for arbitration, would be sufficient to bring home to any one’s mind that the arbitration agreement in the document was being invoked as the basis for arbitration”. He said that clear words were needed to indicate that a dispute is being brought to arbitration “under a specific provision in a particular contract”. Nothing was stated in the notice of arbitration about the dispute resolution clause in the promissory note and therefore, on its face, the notice of arbitration “was only invoking the arbitration clause in the Loan and Amendment Agreements.”

Ryes J 表示，他怀疑“仅仅提及一份文件并在仲裁请求中展示该文件是否足以使任何人意识到该文件中的仲裁协议被援引为仲裁的基础” ”。他表示，需要明确的措辞表明争议正在“根据特定合同的具体条款”提交仲裁。仲裁通知中并未提及本票中的争议解决条款，因此从表面上看，仲裁通知“只是援引了贷款协议和修改协议中的仲裁条款”。 ”

Separability

The concept of separability means that the validity of the arbitration clause does not depend on the validity of the remaining parts of the contract in which it is contained. As long as the arbitration clause itself is validly entered into by the parties and worded sufficiently broadly to cover non-contractual disputes, an arbitrator may declare a contract invalid but still retain jurisdiction to decide a dispute as to the consequences of the invalidity. By treating arbitration agreements as distinct from the main contract, separability rescues many arbitration agreements from failing simply because they are contained in contracts the validity of which is questioned.

分离概念意味着仲裁条款的有效性不依赖于合同其他部分的有效性。只要仲裁条款本身是由当事人有效订立的，并且措辞足够宽泛以涵盖非合同争议，仲裁员可以宣布合同无效，但仍保留管辖权来决定无效的后果。通过将仲裁协议视为独立于主合同，分离原则拯救了许多由于主合同的有效性受到质疑而可能无效的仲裁协议。

Jurisdiction

In an arbitration context, jurisdiction refers to the authority of an arbitral tribunal to make a decision affecting the merits of the case. If a tribunal concludes it has jurisdiction, then it must proceed to rule on the merits of the claim, which may include considering questions of admissibility.

在仲裁领域，管辖权是指仲裁庭做出影响案件实质的决定的权力。如果仲裁员认为其没有管辖权，则无法根据案情作出裁决。如果仲裁庭认定其拥有管辖权，则必须对索赔的是非曲直作出裁决，其中可能包括考虑可否受理问题。

Liability

In arbitration, liability refers to the legal responsibility of a party for their actions or omissions.

在仲裁中，责任是指一方当事人对其作为或不作为承担的法律责任。

In arbitration, there is a distinction between jurisdiction and substantive liability. An entity may be a party to an arbitration agreement even if it did not sign the agreement, but this does not mean that it needs to bear responsibility in the substantive dispute. Conversely, an entity may need to bear responsibility in the substantive dispute but is not necessarily bound by the arbitration agreement. The arbitration agreement and the underlying contract are independent of each other, and an entity may be a party to the arbitration agreement without being a party to the underlying contract. Additionally, the applicable laws may have different criteria for jurisdiction and substantive liability.

在仲裁中，管辖权和实质性责任之间是有区别的。一个实体可能会成为仲裁协议的一方，即使它没有签署该协议，但这并不意味着它在实际争议中需要承担责任。相反，一个实体在实际争议中可能需要承担责任，但不一定受仲裁协议的约束。仲裁协议和基础合同是独立的，一个实体可能是仲裁协议的一方，但不一定是基础合同的一方。而且，适用法律对管辖权和实质性责任可能有不同的标准。

Provisions on the limitation of arbitrators’ liability can be found in most commonly used arbitration rules, for example the ICC Rules (Article 41), the NAI Rules (Article 61), the LCIA Rules (Article 31.1), the SIAC Rules (Article 38) and the HKIAC Rules (Article 46).

关于仲裁员责任限制的规定可以在最常用的仲裁规则中找到，例如《ICC规则》（第41条）、《NAI规则》（第61条）、《LCIA规则》（第31.1条）、《SIAC规则》（第38条） ）和香港国际仲裁中心规则（第 46 条）。

  • Some jurisdictions like France impose liability for failure to disclose conflict of interest.

  • Failure by an arbitrator to comply with their contractual obligations could in theory lead to civil liability. Civil liability exists in very grave cases. 仲裁员未能履行其合同义务理论上可能导致民事责任，民事责任存在于非常严重的情况下。

  • 香港：Provisions limiting liability of Tribunals (ss. 104-105)

  • Most arbitration institution rules provide for the immunity of arbitrators against civil liability. This means that arbitrators cannot be held personally liable for any acts or omissions made during their duties related to arbitration. This immunity is designed to protect arbitrators and ensure that they can make decisions impartially and without fear of personal repercussions. 大多数仲裁机构的规则都规定仲裁员对民事责任免疫。这意味着仲裁员在执行与仲裁相关的职责过程中，因其行为或疏忽不会承担个人责任。这种免疫旨在保护仲裁员，确保他们能够公正地作出决定，而不必担心个人后果。

    • For Ad Hoc Arbitration: An agreement may be necessary to specify the extent of civil liability for the arbitrators. 对于临时仲裁：可能需要通过协议明确仲裁员民事责任的范围。
    • 2017 ICC Rules Art 41: This article states that arbitrators, any person appointed by the arbitral tribunal, the emergency arbitrator, the Court and its members, the ICC and its employees, and the ICC National Committees and Groups and their employees and representatives shall not be liable to any person for any act or omission related to the arbitration, except where such limitation of liability is prohibited by applicable law. 2017年国际商会仲裁规则第41条：该条款规定，仲裁员、仲裁庭任命的任何人、紧急仲裁员、法院及其成员、国际商会及其员工、国际商会国家委员会和小组及其员工和代表因与仲裁相关的任何行为或疏忽，不对任何人承担责任，除非适用法律禁止此类责任限制。

Merits

The term merits refer to the substantive aspects of the arbitrator’s decision. This includes the actual issues in dispute, the evidence presented, and the reasoning and conclusions reached by the arbitrator. “实质内容”一词是指仲裁员决定的实质性方面。这包括争议的实际问题、提供的证据以及仲裁员得出的推理和结论。

When it is stated that there is “no judicial review of the merits,” it means that courts will not re-examine or second-guess the substantive decisions made by the arbitrator. Instead, the courts will only review the procedural aspects of arbitration, such as whether the process was fair and in accordance with the agreed arbitration rules, rather than whether the arbitrator made the “right” decision based on the facts and law of the case.

当提到“不对案情进行司法审查”时，意味着法院不会重新审查或事后猜测仲裁员做出的实质性决定。相反，法院只会审查仲裁的程序方面，例如程序是否公平、是否符合约定的仲裁规则，而不是仲裁员是否根据案件事实和法律做出了“正确”的决定。 。

This principle supports the finality and efficiency of arbitration, ensuring that the arbitrator’s decision is respected and not subject to lengthy judicial scrutiny.

这一原则支持仲裁的终局性和效率，确保仲裁员的决定得到尊重且不受冗长的司法审查。

  • In considering whether or not to refuse the enforcement of the award, the court does not look into the merits or at the underlying transaction (Xiamen Xingjingdi Group Ltd v Eton Properties Limited [2009] 4 HKLRD 353 (CA)).
  • Many jurisdictions no longer allow courts to review the substantive content of arbitration awards in order to protect the independence and finality of arbitration. However, some jurisdictions still permit the annulment of arbitration awards based on the merits of the decision. These jurisdictions include England, Ireland, China, Australia, Singapore, Abu Dhabi, Libya, Saudi Arabia, Egypt, and the United States. 许多司法管辖区不再允许法院审查仲裁裁决的实质性内容，以保护仲裁的独立性和终局性。但是，一些司法管辖区仍然允许根据裁决的是非曲直撤销仲裁裁决。这些司法管辖区包括英格兰、爱尔兰、中国、澳大利亚、新加坡、阿布扎比、利比亚、沙特阿拉伯、埃及和美国。

Quantum

Quantum is the amount of damages that are awarded to a successful party in a claim.

The quantum phase involves assessing the amount of damages to be awarded against the respondent. In complex commercial disputes, this often requires detailed expert accounting evidence from the parties. The tribunal typically splits the hearing into liability and quantum phases. By determining liability before considering the question of damages, the tribunal aims to avoid the cost to the parties of obtaining expert evidence if the respondent is found not to be liable.

量化阶段是评估应向被申请人裁定的损害赔偿金额。在复杂的商业纠纷中，这通常需要当事人提供详尽的专家会计证据。仲裁庭通常将听证会分为责任阶段和量化阶段。通过先确定责任问题，再考虑损害赔偿问题，仲裁庭旨在避免如果被申请人未被认定承担责任时，当事人获得这些专家证据的成本。

Admissibility

In the context of arbitration, “jurisdiction” refers to the authority of an arbitral tribunal to make a decision affecting the merits of the case. If an arbitrator decides it has no jurisdiction, it cannot make an award on the merits.

在仲裁领域，“管辖权”指仲裁庭做出影响案件实质性决定的权力。如果仲裁员决定其没有管辖权，则无法对案件实质做出裁决。

“Admissibility,” on the other hand, refers to the tribunal’s power to decide a case at a particular point in time, considering any possible temporary or permanent defects in the claim. Jurisdiction pertains to the power of the tribunal to hear a case, while admissibility concerns whether it is appropriate for the tribunal to hear it at that time.

而“可受理性”指仲裁庭在特定时间判断案件的权力，考虑到可能存在的临时或永久性缺陷。管辖权涉及仲裁庭审理案件的权力，可受理性则是仲裁庭在该时间点审理是否合适。

The distinction between jurisdiction and admissibility can be complex and may vary depending on legal perspectives or the specific laws governing the arbitration. Challenges to the tribunal typically raise jurisdictional issues, while challenges to the claim itself raise issues of admissibility. If a tribunal concludes it has jurisdiction, it must proceed to rule on the merits, including considering questions of admissibility.

管辖权和可受理性之间的区别可能很复杂，且可能因法律视角和具体适用的仲裁法律而异。对仲裁庭的质疑通常涉及管辖权问题，而对案件本身的质疑则涉及可受理性问题。如果仲裁庭认定其有管辖权，则必须继续对案件实质进行裁决，包括考虑可受理性问题。

Jan Paulsson highlighted that while it may be difficult to precisely define the dividing line between admissibility and jurisdiction, it is still possible to determine which side a particular claim falls on. Decisions on jurisdiction are usually reviewable by courts, whereas decisions on the admissibility of a claim, once the parties have consented to arbitration, should be final and binding. If a tribunal dismisses a claim as inadmissible, the claimant can resubmit it after addressing the defect that caused the inadmissibility.

Jan Paulsson指出，虽然确定可受理性和管辖权之间的确切界线可能不容易，但仍然可以确定特定索赔属于哪一边。有关管辖权的决定通常可以由法院复审，而对索赔可受理性的判断，一旦当事人同意仲裁，应是最终且有约束力的。如果仲裁庭以可受理性问题驳回索赔，申请人可以在解决导致不受理的问题后重新提交索赔。

C v D: Hong Kong in Step with the Admissibility Versus Jurisdiction Debate

Various jurisdictions, such as the UK, US, and Singapore, recognize the differences between admissibility and jurisdiction in arbitration, extensively covered in scholarly work. The Hong Kong Court of Appeal’s decision in the case of C v D marks an important judicial development by confirming that pre-arbitration procedural requirements are issues of admissibility, thereby preventing subsequent court review.

英国、美国、新加坡等多个司法管辖区都认识到仲裁中可受理性与管辖权的区别，并在学术界广泛讨论。香港上诉法院在C诉D案中的裁决是一个重要的司法发展，确认了仲裁庭对于仲裁前程序要求的决定权，将其视为可受理性问题，从而排除了法院的后续审查。

Pre-arbitration conditions sometimes require parties to use alternative dispute resolution methods (e.g., negotiation, mediation) before arbitration. The distinction between admissibility (whether bringing a claim is appropriate) and jurisdiction (tribunal’s power to decide) is crucial. Jan Paulsson’s “tribunal versus claim” test explains that objections affecting forum consent target jurisdiction, while those about claim defects target admissibility.

仲裁前条件有时要求当事人在仲裁前使用替代性争议解决方法（如协商、调解）。区分可受理性（是否适合提交仲裁庭）和管辖权（仲裁庭是否有权裁决）非常重要。Jan Paulsson的“仲裁庭对抗索赔”测试解释了，影响仲裁协议的异议涉及管辖权，而有关索赔缺陷的异议则涉及可受理性。

The Court of Appeal in C v D held that the fulfillment of pre-arbitration procedural requirements (e.g., negotiation) is a question of admissibility, not jurisdiction. This aligns with international practice, distinguishing between claims’ admissibility and jurisdiction. The case involved a dispute over the development of a satellite, where pre-arbitration negotiation was mandated. The tribunal ruled that negotiation had occurred, rejecting C’s jurisdictional objections.

香港上诉法院在C诉D案中认为，是否履行了仲裁前程序要求（如协商）是一个可受理性问题，而非管辖权问题。这符合国际惯例，区分了索赔的可受理性和管辖权。此案涉及卫星开发的争议，合同规定必须先进行协商。仲裁庭裁定已经进行了协商，驳回了C的管辖权异议。

C sought to set aside the tribunal’s award, citing jurisdictional issues under Hong Kong’s Arbitration Ordinance, which mirrors the Model Law. The Court of First Instance and the Court of Appeal confirmed that procedural pre-arbitration conditions are issues of admissibility. This decision solidifies that questions of procedural compliance are for the tribunal to decide and not for court review.

C据香港《仲裁条例》提出撤销仲裁裁决的请求，理由是管辖权问题。香港法院一审和上诉法院都确认程序性仲裁前条件是可受理性问题，应由仲裁庭决定，而非法院审查。

Gary Born suggests that parties prefer arbitration as a centralized forum, making it suitable for deciding on pre-arbitrational procedural compliance, which pertains to admissibility, not jurisdiction. Distinguishing between the two is crucial as it determines whether issues are subject to court review. The judgment in C v D enhances Hong Kong’s pro-arbitration regime by promoting party autonomy, limiting court intervention, and achieving efficient dispute resolution.

Gary Born认为，当事人倾向于将仲裁作为集中解决争议的地方，仲裁庭更适合决定仲裁前程序要求的履行，这涉及可受理性而非管辖权。区分两者非常重要，因为它决定了问题是否需要法院审查。C诉D案的判决增强了香港的亲仲裁制度，促进了当事人的自主权，限制了法院的干预，实现了高效的争议解决。

T v B

In so doing, the Court reaffirmed the principle that compliance with pre-conditions to arbitration is a question of admissibility, not jurisdiction, and that an arbitral tribunal’s decision on admissibility is beyond the purview of the Hong Kong courts.

在近期T v B [2021] HKCFI 3645一案的判决中，香港高等法院指出，“如果法院是其程序规则的主人，那么仲裁庭也应如此”。法院在此过程中重申了以下原则：遵守仲裁的先决条件是一个可否受理的问题，而不是管辖权的问题，仲裁庭对可否受理的决定不属于香港法院的职权范围。

The Court’s judgment applies the principle laid down in the landmark decision of C v D [2021] HKCFI 1474.

法院的判决适用了具有里程碑意义的C v D [2021] HKCFI 1474判决中规定的原则。

The case involved a contractor and subcontractor who entered into a works agreement with a multi-tiered arbitration clause. The clause here was different from the two English cases above in that, instead of requiring mediation, it prohibited arbitration until completion of the works. The defendant served a Notice of Dispute on the claimant before the project had completed and, as a result, the claimant argued that the Defendant had done so in breach of the terms of their agreement.

香港对此问题的最新判决是T v B ，涉及承包商和分包商签订了包含多层仲裁条款的工程协议。该条款与上述两个英国案例的不同之处在于，它不要求调解，而是在工程完成之前禁止仲裁。被告在项目完成之前向原告发出了争议通知，因此原告辩称被告这样做违反了协议条款。

The Court upheld the judgment in C v D, ruling that whether pre-arbitration conditions had been fulfilled was a matter of admissibility, not jurisdiction, even though the parties and the arbitrator had referred to it as a ‘jurisdictional challenge’. The Court noted that this distinction 法院维持了C诉D案中的最新判决，裁定仲裁前条件是否已履行是可受理性问题，而非管辖权问题，即使当事人和仲裁员已将其称为“管辖权挑战”。法院指出，这一区别:

  1. Makes conceptual sense, 在概念上是合理的
  2. Respects party autonomy, 尊重当事人的自主权
  3. Aligns with the trend of judicial restraint in arbitration, 符合司法对仲裁程序的克制干预趋势
  4. Supports the Arbitration Ordinance’s aim of fair and speedy dispute resolution, 支持《仲裁条例》公平快速解决争议的目标
  5. Aligns Hong Kong with the international arbitration community. 使香港与国际仲裁界接轨

Arbitral awards on the admissibility of claims cannot be challenged under section 81 of the Arbitration Ordinance. Therefore, the Court dismissed T’s application to set aside the award. The Court also noted that just as it is the master of its own procedural rules, so should be the arbitral tribunal. A tribunal’s decision on compliance with pre-arbitration procedures or conditions should be final and non-reviewable by the Court.

关于可受理性问题的仲裁裁决不能根据《仲裁条例》第81条进行挑战。因此，法院驳回了T的撤销裁决申请。法院还指出，就像法院是自身程序规则的主宰者一样，仲裁庭也应如此。仲裁庭关于当事人是否遵守仲裁前程序或条件的决定应是最终的，并且不受法院审查。

It is notable that this is the third Hong Kong case, following C v D and Kinli Civil Engineering Limited v Geotech Engineering Limited [2021] HKCFI 2503, where the Hong Kong courts have upheld this principle. The upholding of this principle in these judgments is also consistent with the recent decisions of courts in other common law jurisdictions, such as England and Wales (see NWA v NVF [2021] EWHC 2666 (Comm)) and Australia (New South Wales) (see Nuance Group (Australia) Pty Ltd v Shape Australia Pty Ltd [2021] NSWSC 1498).

Setting Aside

Setting an award aside means that it is ignored as invalid. The award is stopped and the matter again becomes available for judgement. The parties are entitled to return to arbitration or to have the matter resolved by a court of law.

Applications to set aside an award, based on fraud or otherwise, may be made pursuant to section 81 of the HKAO. The grounds for setting aside an award include incapacity of a party, invalidity of the arbitration agreement, inability to present a party’s case, arbitrability and conflict with Hong Kong public policy.

Enforcement

Usually, enforcement constitutes the “process of obtaining an order by a court or authority directing compliance in accordance with the award.” As stressed in Redfern and Hunter on International Arbitration, enforcement “goes a step further than recognition. In contrast with recognition, enforcement is used as a “sword […] applying legal sanctions to compel the party against whom the award was made to carry it out.”

Under Hong Kong law, the first step towards the recognition and enforcement of an arbitral award is obtaining the Court’s grant of leave to enforce the award.

根据香港法律，承认和执行仲裁裁决的第一步是获得法院批准执行该裁决。

The procedure for seeking leave to enforce an award under section 84 is governed by Order 73, Rule 10 of the RHC. The application is usually made ex parte, and the applicant must make full and frank disclosure of all relevant information in support of the application, including the existence of any proceedings to set aside the award.

根据第 84 条寻求执行裁决许可的程序受 RHC 第 73 号命令第 10 条的管辖。申请通常是单方面提出的，申请人必须充分、坦诚地披露支持申请的所有相关信息，包括是否存在任何撤销裁决的程序。

Recognition

Recognition in international arbitration aims to acknowledge that the arbitral award is final and binding and has a res judicata effect. Recognition in international arbitration is used as a “shield [to] block any attempt to raise in fresh proceedings issues that have already been decided in the arbitration”.

国际仲裁中的承认旨在承认仲裁裁决是终局的、具有约束力并具有既判力的效力。国际仲裁中的承认被用作“阻止任何试图在新的程序中提出仲裁中已决定的问题的尝试”。

Recognition of an arbitral award essentially means that it is accepted as valid and can produce the same effects as a domestic court judgment. 承认仲裁裁决实质上意味着该裁决被接受为有效，并能产生与国内法院判决相同的效力。

Due Process

The concept of due process requires that each party is given notice of the proceedings and the case against them, treated equally, and provided a reasonable opportunity to present their case before an impartial tribunal. Under the New York Convention, due process violations are grounds for setting aside an award to protect parties against procedural unfairness and uphold policies of fundamental importance to the country. To avoid awards being set aside, arbitrators must act judicially, respecting due process rules.

正当程序的概念要求每一方都应得到诉讼通知及其对方的案情，受到平等对待，并有合理的机会在公正的仲裁庭前陈述其案情。根据《纽约公约》，违反正当程序的情况是撤销裁决的理由，以保护当事人免受程序不公和维护国家的基本政策。为了避免裁决被撤销，仲裁员必须遵循正当程序规则，公正行事并被视为公正行事。

Common law principles of natural justice or procedural fairness comprise two main aspects in legal proceedings. The first is the right of a party to prior notice and an effective opportunity to make representations before a decision is made. The second is the right of the affected party to an unbiased tribunal. These principles are modified, codified, and included in the Model Law, as well as national and international arbitration laws. The first principle, often referred to as equal treatment of parties, ensures they have a full and reasonable opportunity to present their cases. The second principle requires the tribunal to be impartial and independent.

普通法的自然公正或程序公正原则包括法律诉讼中的两个主要方面。第一是当事人在决策前有权获得事先通知和有效的陈述机会。第二是受影响的一方有权获得一个公正的审判庭。这些原则经过修改，纳入《示范法》以及国家和国际仲裁法律。第一原则，通常称为对当事人的平等待遇，确保他们有充分和合理的机会陈述其案情。第二原则要求仲裁庭必须公正和独立。

纽约公约

The New York Convention, formally known as the Convention on the Recognition and Enforcement of Foreign Arbitral Awards, was adopted by the United Nations on June 10, 1958. It is one of the most important international treaties in the field of international arbitration. The Convention facilitates the recognition and enforcement of arbitral awards in the signatory countries, significantly simplifying and streamlining the process across borders.

ICSID Convention

The ICSID Convention, formally known as the Convention on the Settlement of Investment Disputes between States and Nationals of Other States, was established by the International Centre for Settlement of Investment Disputes (ICSID) under the auspices of the World Bank. The Convention was signed on March 18, 1965, and came into force on October 14, 1966.

The ICSID Convention is designed to facilitate and promote the resolution of investment disputes between host states and foreign investors. It provides a comprehensive legal framework for the conduct of arbitration and conciliation proceedings, thereby encouraging international investment by creating a stable and predictable mechanism for dispute resolution.

Grounds to Set Aside

Applications to set aside an award, based on fraud or otherwise, may be made pursuant to section 81 of the HKAO. The grounds for setting aside an award include incapacity of a party, invalidity of the arbitration agreement, inability to present a party’s case, arbitrability and conflict with Hong Kong public policy. The Court will not consider the merits of the dispute or the correctness of the award.

基于欺诈或其他原因，可以根据 HKAO 第 81 条提出撤销裁决的申请。撤销裁决的理由包括当事人无行为能力、仲裁协议无效、无法陈述当事人的案件、可仲裁性以及与香港公共政策相冲突。法院不会考虑争议的实质或裁决的正确性。

An application to set aside an award must be made within three months of the date on which the party making the application received the award (HKAO, section 81, paragraph (1)(3)). If an application has been made for correction and interpretation of an award, an application to set it aside must be made within three months from the date on which the tribunal disposed of the request. (HKAO, section 81, paragraph (1)(3)).

撤销裁决的申请必须在提出申请的一方收到裁决之日起三个月内提出（HKAO，第 81 条，第 (1)(3) 段）。如果已提出更正和解释裁决的申请，则必须在仲裁庭处理该请求之日起三个月内提出撤销裁决的申请。

In the case of LY v HW, [2022] HKCFI 2267, the Hong Kong Court dismissed an application to set aside an arbitration award. The application was based on claims that the tribunal had failed to address key issues and had not provided sufficient reasons for its decision. This decision emphasizes the strict and narrow interpretation of grounds for refusing enforcement of arbitration awards in Hong Kong, thereby strengthening their enforceability. 在LY诉HW案，[2022] HKCFI 2267中，香港法院驳回了撤销仲裁裁决的申请。申请理由是仲裁庭未处理关键问题且未充分说明其决定理由。此裁决强调了严格且狭隘解释拒绝执行仲裁裁决的理由，从而强化了仲裁裁决在香港的执行力。

  • Narrow Interpretation : The Court referred to previous decisions that interpreted the public policy ground narrowly, setting aside awards only in cases of serious errors causing substantial injustice.
  • Due Process : Violations of due process are only acknowledged in serious cases involving egregious errors.
  • Limited Grounds : The grounds for refusing enforcement are limited and must be narrowly construed.
  • Improper Challenges : Parties cannot seek to set aside an award simply to reargue points that were ignored or briefly addressed by the tribunal.
  • Errors of Law : An award cannot be set aside based on an error of law unless it results in a breach of natural justice or failure to follow the agreed arbitral procedure. Only egregious errors causing substantial injustice warrant setting aside.

Grounds to Refuse Enforcement

The major grounds for refusing recognition and enforcement of an arbitral award in Hong Kong are set out under sections 86(1), 89(2), 95(2) and 98D(2) of the HKAO, which substantially replicate the grounds set out in article V(1) of the Convention.

  • incapacity of the parties or invalidity of the arbitration agreement;
  • violation of due process rules;
  • differences not falling within the terms of, or decisions on matters beyond the scope of, the submission to arbitration;
  • improper composition of the arbitral authority or non-respect of arbitral procedure; and
  • award not yet binding, set aside or suspended; and

Passive/Active Remedy

Two options for a party against whom an award was rendered: (i) an “active remedy” of setting aside the award; or (ii) a “passive remedy” of resisting enforcement by the counterparty, which was available even where no active challenge had been made.

The “Choice of Remedies” Doctrine pertains to a party’s ability to choose from multiple avenues of legal recourse when dealing with arbitration awards, particularly in disputes involving international arbitration. This doctrine allows a party to either challenge an arbitration award at the seat of arbitration or resist its enforcement in another jurisdiction without necessarily having challenged it at the seat.

选择救济原则涉及当事人在处理仲裁裁决时，特别是涉及国际仲裁的争议时，从多种法律追索途径中进行选择的能力。该原则允许当事人在仲裁地对仲裁裁决提出质疑，或者在另一个司法管辖区抵制仲裁裁决的执行，而不必在仲裁地提出质疑。

In Astro Nusantra International BV v PT Ayunda (2018) 21 HKCFAR 118, the plaintiffs (Ps) obtained an arbitration award in Singapore (SIAC) against the defendants (Ds). In Singapore, the plaintiffs initially succeeded in obtaining leave to enforce the award, but later, the Singapore Court of Appeal (SGCA) set aside the enforcement order. In Hong Kong, the plaintiffs obtained leave to enforce the award under the old Hong Kong Arbitration Ordinance (HKAO). The defendants did not oppose the enforcement order within the 14-day period. Later, the defendants sought an extension of time to resist enforcement. The proceedings went all the way to the Court of Final Appeal (CFA), which allowed the defendants’ appeal and granted an extension of time.

原告（Ps）在新加坡国际仲裁中心（SIAC）对被告（Ds）获得仲裁裁决。在新加坡，原告最初成功获得执行令，但后来新加坡上诉法院（SGCA）撤销了该执行令。在香港，原告根据旧版《香港仲裁条例》（HKAO）获得了执行令。被告在14天的期限内并未反对执行令，后来被告申请延长时间以反对执行令。诉讼一直上诉到终审法院（CFA），终审法院允许被告的上诉并同意延长期限。

  • Convention Flexibility: The case cited the approval of Dallah Real Estate and Tourism Holding Co v Ministry of Religious Affairs of the Government of Pakistan [2011] 1 AC 763 at p 837, stating that there is nothing in the New York Convention obligating a party resisting an award on the ground of the non-existence of an arbitration agreement to challenge the award before the courts of the seat of arbitration.
    • 公约的灵活性： 案例中引用并赞同了Dallah Real Estate and Tourism Holding Co诉巴基斯坦宗教事务部[2011] 1 AC 763第837页的判决，指出《纽约公约》中没有任何规定要求抗辩仲裁协议不存在的当事方必须在仲裁地法院挑战裁决。
  • Section 44(2) Consistency: Section 44(2) (now Section 89) of the HKAO aligns with the choice of remedies principle, enabling the concerned party to resist enforcement in Hong Kong without having challenged the award in the supervisory court. The CFA found that the lower courts’ decisions to refuse the extension of time based on the fact that the awards were not set aside in Singapore conflicted with this principle.
    • 第44(2)条（现为第89条）与选择救济原则一致，使相关方即使未在监督法院挑战裁决也可以在香港抗辩执行。终审法院发现，下级法院因裁决未在新加坡被撤销而拒绝延长时间的裁决，与选择救济原则相冲突。
  • Implication: This case sets a precedent in Hong Kong, affirming that parties can resist the enforcement of an arbitration award in Hong Kong without having challenged the award in the supervisory jurisdiction.
    • 此案例在香港确立了一个先例，确认当事方可以在未在监督司法管辖区挑战裁决的情况下，在香港抗辩执行仲裁裁决。

Public Policy

Party autonomy is at the core of international arbitration. However, it has its limits. Two of the most notable limitations to party autonomy are on grounds of arbitrability and public policy.

当事人意思自治是国际仲裁的核心。然而，它也有其局限性。对当事人意思自治的两个最显着的限制是基于可仲裁性和公共政策。

Neither the Model Law (which many jurisdictions base their domestic arbitration laws on) nor the New York Convention provide a definition of public policy. 《示范法》（许多司法管辖区以其国内仲裁法为基础）和《纽约公约》均未提供公共政策的定义。

Consequently, states have developed their own definitions of public policy through legislation or jurisprudence. Typically, these definitions are influenced by each state’s fundamental economic, religious, social, and political standards. Courts worldwide review awards based on the core values of their legal systems or local standards of morality, justice, and the public interest. This approach aims to balance the parties’ right to autonomy with the state’s interest in preserving fundamental values.

因此，各国通过立法或判例制定了自己的公共政策定义。通常，这些定义受各国基本经济、宗教、社会和政治标准的影响。世界各地的法院根据其法律体系的核心价值观或当地的道德、正义和公共利益标准来审查裁决。这种方式旨在平衡当事人的自治权和国家在维护基本价值观方面的利益。

According to the International Law Association, public policy exceptions include infringements of mandatory rules, breaches of fundamental principles of law, actions contrary to good morals, and actions contrary to national interests. However, there is no uniform or universally accepted definition of ‘public policy.’ 根据国际法协会的说法，公共政策例外包括违反强制性规则、违反法律基本原则、违背良好道德的行为和违反国家利益的行为。然而，不可能对“公共政策”提供一个统一且普遍接受的定义。

Moreover, public policy encompasses fundamental norms that no court can depart from, going beyond the concept of ‘mandatory laws.’ Rules on competition law, bankruptcy, consumer protection, offshore transactions, foreign exchange, and export prohibitions are often seen as mandatory and need consideration when reviewing, recognizing, or enforcing an arbitral award, provided the dispute involves these laws. However, not all mandatory laws fall within the scope of public policy, only clear and serious violations resulting in a conflict with fundamental notions of decency and justice.

此外，公共政策包含法院不能背离的基本规范，超越了“强制性法律”的概念。竞争法、破产法、消费者保护、离岸期货交易、外汇和出口禁令等规则通常被视为强制性法律，并在审查、承认或执行仲裁裁决时需要考虑这些规则，前提是争议涉及这些法律。然而，并非所有的强制性法律都属于公共政策的范畴，只有非常明显和严重违反强制性法律并导致与体面和公正的基本概念发生冲突的情况才会这样做。

Infra Petita

Infra Petita refers to a situation in arbitration where the arbitral tribunal has rendered an award that falls short of addressing all the issues or claims presented by the parties. Essentially, it means “less than requested” and implies that the tribunal has failed to fully resolve the dispute as presented in the arbitration proceedings. This can be a ground for challenging or setting aside the arbitral award as it indicates that not all matters submitted for arbitration were considered.

Infra Petita指的是在仲裁中，仲裁庭作出的裁决没有解决当事人提出的所有问题或请求。这实际上意味着“少于请求”，表明仲裁庭未能完全解决仲裁程序中提出的争议。这可能成为挑战或撤销仲裁裁决的理由，因为这表明并非所有提交仲裁的事项都得到了考虑。

Ultra Petita

Ultra Petita, on the other hand, refers to a situation where the arbitral tribunal has exceeded its authority by making an award that addresses issues or grants relief that go beyond what was requested by the parties. Essentially, it means “more than requested” and implies that the tribunal has gone beyond the scope of the arbitration agreement and the matters submitted for decision. This can also be a ground for challenging or setting aside the arbitral award as it indicates that the tribunal has overstepped its jurisdiction.

Ultra Petita则指的是仲裁庭超出了其权限，作出裁决涉及的事项或给予的救济超出了当事人所请求的范围。这实际上意味着“超出请求”，表明仲裁庭超出了仲裁协议的范围以及提交决议的事项。这也可能成为挑战或撤销仲裁裁决的理由，因为这表明仲裁庭超出了其管辖权。

Applicable Law

Determining the applicable law is an important step in an arbitration proceeding. It is a complex issue arbitral tribunals have to deal with in investor-State disputes in which many legal rules can interconnect, whether international and/or domestic, on the same or several stages of the procedure.

确定适用的法律是仲裁程序的重要一步。这是仲裁庭在投资者与国家争端中必须处理的一个复杂问题，其中许多法律规则可以在程序的相同或多个阶段相互关联，无论是国际和/或国内的。

In its broadest sense, the term “applicable law” could include one or more of the following questions:

从最广泛的意义上来说，“适用法律”一词可能包括以下一个或多个问题：

  • Substantive applicable law to the arbitration clause; 仲裁条款的实体适用法；
  • Substantive applicable law to the merits of the dispute; 争议实质适用的实体法律；
  • Procedural applicable law to the proceedings; and 诉讼程序适用的程序法；和
  • Choice of law rules that apply in selecting these laws. 选择这些法律时适用的法律选择规则。

Governing Law

The law governing the arbitration agreement covers substantive matters relating to the agreement to arbitrate, for example, the interpretation, scope and validity of the agreement to arbitrate.

Enforcement Jurisdiction

Enforcement jurisdiction refers to the legal authority of a court in a specific jurisdiction to recognize and enforce an arbitral award. This jurisdiction is crucial because it determines where a successful party in arbitration can seek the enforcement of an award, especially in cases where the losing party has assets.

执行管辖权是指特定司法管辖区的法院对承认和执行仲裁裁决的法律权力。这一管辖权至关重要，因为它决定了仲裁中成功方可以在何处寻求执行裁决，特别是在败诉方拥有资产的情况下。

  • Recognition and Enforcement : Recognition means that the court acknowledges the arbitral award as valid and binding. Enforcement means that the court takes steps to compel the losing party to comply with the award. 承认是指法院确认仲裁裁决有效且具有约束力。执行是指法院采取措施强制败诉方遵守裁决。
  • Jurisdiction : The court must have jurisdiction over either the losing party or the assets located within its territory.
