This is typically in the country where the assets of the losing party are located, ensuring that the award can be satisfied. 法院必须对败诉方或其资产所在的领土具有管辖权。通常，这在败诉方资产所在的国家，以确保裁决能够得到履行。

Validity of Arbitration Agreement

According to Article 7 of the UNCITRAL Model Law and Section 19 of the Arbitration Ordinance, an arbitration agreement is an agreement to submit disputes related to a defined legal relationship to arbitration. It can be part of a contract or a separate agreement and must be in writing.

Valid arbitration agreements must expressly state the parties’ intention to arbitrate. Language such as “shall” indicates compulsion, while terms like “may” can lead to disputes over the mandatory nature of arbitration.

The scope of the arbitration clause should clearly define which disputes are to be resolved through arbitration. Courts typically favor a pro-arbitration stance, interpreting clauses to include as many types of disputes as possible.

Some clauses may require parties to attempt negotiation before arbitration. Failure to meet such preconditions typically concerns the admissibility of the arbitration, which is for the tribunal to decide, not a court. The governing law for the arbitration agreement may differ from the governing law of the contract and the seat of arbitration. Determining the appropriate law involves examining explicit or implied choices by the parties and the jurisdiction most closely connected to the agreement.

It is important for businesses to draft clear and precise arbitration clauses to avoid disputes over validity. Legal assistance is recommended to navigate the complexities and ensure enforceability of such clauses.

The validity of an arbitration agreement encompasses both formal and substantive validity. The most common requirement for the written form of international arbitration agreements is found in the New York Convention. According to Article II(1), the Convention applies only to “an agreement in writing,” which is defined in Article II(2) to include an arbitration clause in a contract or an arbitration agreement signed by the parties or contained in an exchange of letters or telegrams. Most national arbitration laws impose some form of written requirement for arbitration agreements. Many domestic laws align with Article II(2) of the Convention, while incorporating modern elements such as emails and other electronic communications.

Like other contracts, arbitration agreements also raise issues of substantive validity. The types of arbitration agreements deemed invalid under the New York Convention and most domestic laws are generally limited to scenarios under common contract law principles (e.g., mistake, fraud, unconscionability, waiver). These grounds for challenging the substantive validity of arbitration agreements are exclusive exceptions to their presumptive validity.

Moreover, certain types of disputes are explicitly deemed non-arbitrable by law. These exceptions are outlined in Article II(1) and Article V(2)(a) of the New York Convention, which specify certain matters that cannot be resolved through arbitration. These non-arbitrable matters will be discussed separately below.

Independence and Impartiality

Independence refers to the objective and external manifestations of the relationships between the parties, counsels, and co-arbitrators. An arbitrator shall not only be independent but must also be perceived as independent by third parties. Impartiality is generally a subjective and abstract concept, referring to an arbitrator’s state of mind and discernible from their external conduct. It involves an “absence of external control” as well as any “bias and predisposition towards a party.” Some arbitration rules initially did not explicitly list impartiality as grounds for challenging an arbitrator but have since been amended to include it. ICSID tribunals reviewing arbitrator challenges have explicitly recognized that independence and impartiality are the two “key qualifications of arbitrators” and that a manifest lack of these qualifications constitutes a valid ground for challenging an arbitrator.

独立性是指当事各方、律师和共同仲裁员之间的关系在客观和外部表现上的独立。仲裁员不仅需要独立，还应被第三方视为独立的。仲裁员的公正性通常是指一种主观和抽象的心态概念，难以衡量，可以从其外部行为中推断。其包括“外部控制的缺失”以及对一方的“偏见和倾向”。一些仲裁规则最初没有明确列出公正性作为质疑仲裁员的理由，但已被修订以包括公正性。审查仲裁员质疑的ICSID仲裁庭明确承认独立性和公正性是仲裁员的两个“关键资格”，显然缺乏这些资格构成对仲裁员提出质疑的有效理由。

A common requirement in most arbitration rules and national laws is that an arbitrator must act impartially and independently, disclosing any relevant circumstances to maintain the necessary perception of their independence and impartiality. A lack of independence or impartiality may be grounds for challenging an arbitrator or the tribunal’s award. However, the standards for impartiality and independence can vary between different arbitration institutions and seats of arbitration. For instance, English courts often apply the “real danger of bias” test, while US law mandates that an arbitrator must avoid “evident partiality.”

大多数仲裁规则和国家法律中普遍的要求是，仲裁员必须公正和独立行事，并有义务披露相关情况，以保持必要的独立和公正形象。独立性或公正性的缺失可能成为对仲裁员或仲裁庭裁决提出质疑的理由。然而，公正性和独立性的标准可能因不同的仲裁机构和仲裁地而异。例如，英国法院倾向于采用“现实可能产生偏见”的标准，而美国法律则要求仲裁员必须避免“明显的偏袒”。

Challenge to Arbitrators

A challenge against an arbitrator must demonstrate that the arbitrator is not sufficiently independent, impartial, or suitable to decide the dispute. When a party decides to challenge an arbitrator, it must act promptly. Most institutional rules require a party to raise an objection to the arbitrator soon after they are nominated or upon becoming aware of circumstances requiring recusal, whether due to bias or other reasons. Article 13(1) of the UNCITRAL Arbitration Rules stipulates that a party must notify of the challenge within 15 days of becoming aware of the grounds for recusal. Parties are not allowed to secretly hold back reasons for objection while the arbitration is ongoing. Failure to act promptly results in a waiver.

对仲裁员提出异议必须证明该仲裁员在独立性、公正性或其他方面不适合裁决争议。当一方决定对仲裁员提出异议时，必须迅速行动。大多数机构规则要求当事人在仲裁员被提名或知悉需回避事宜后迅速对仲裁员提出异议，不论是基于缺乏公正性还是其他理由。《联合国国际贸易法委员会仲裁规则》第13条第1款规定，当事人应该在知悉仲裁员需回避事宜后的15日内发出申请回避的通知。当事人不应被允许在进行仲裁程序的同时，秘密保留对裁判者提出异议的理由。如果不迅速提出，将导致弃权。

Institutional vs. ‘ad hoc’ arbitration

An institutional arbitration is one in which a specialised institution intervenes and takes on the role of administering the arbitration process. Each institution has its own set of rules which provide a framework for arbitration, and its own form of administration to assist in the process.

An ad hoc arbitration is one which is not administered by an institution such as the ICC, LCIA, DIAC or DIFC. The parties will therefore have to determine all aspects of the arbitration themselves . For example, the number of arbitrators, appointing those arbitrators, the applicable law and the procedure for conducting the arbitration.

Parties sometimes opt for pre-established procedural rules designed for ad hoc arbitration. For international commercial arbitration, the United Nations Commission on International Trade Law (UNCITRAL) has issued such rules, known as the “UNCITRAL Arbitration Rules” .

In ad hoc arbitration, parties usually agree to appoint a designated institution to select arbitrators if they cannot reach an agreement, and to handle any subsequent challenges to the tribunal members. If parties cannot successfully select a designated institution, many national arbitration laws allow domestic courts to appoint arbitrators. However, court intervention is generally less desirable compared to the appointment by an experienced designated institution.

Arbitral Institution

An arbitral institution is an organization that provides administrative and procedural support for arbitration proceedings. These institutions establish rules and guidelines for conducting arbitration, offer venues, and may appoint arbitrators if the parties cannot agree on one. Some renowned arbitral institutions include the International Chamber of Commerce (ICC), the London Court of International Arbitration (LCIA), and the Hong Kong International Arbitration Centre (HKIAC). Their role is to ensure that the arbitration process is efficient, fair, and impartial, facilitating the resolution of disputes outside of the court system.

仲裁机构是提供仲裁程序的行政和程序支持的组织。这些机构制定进行仲裁的规则和指南，提供场地，并且在当事人无法达成一致时可以指定仲裁员。著名的仲裁机构包括国际商会（ICC）、伦敦国际仲裁院（LCIA）和香港国际仲裁中心（HKIAC）。它们的作用是确保仲裁过程高效、公平和公正，促进在法院系统之外解决争议。

Arbitration Rules

Arbitration rules are a set of guidelines and procedures established by an arbitration institution or adopted by the parties involved in arbitration to govern the conduct of the arbitration proceedings. These rules outline the framework within which arbitration is to take place, including aspects such as the appointment of arbitrators, submission of evidence, the arbitration hearing process, and the issuance of the final award. The rules ensure that the arbitration process is fair, efficient, and predictable.

Parties to Arbitration Agreement:

Parties to an arbitration agreement are those who have explicitly agreed to submit their disputes to arbitration, typically by signing the arbitration agreement. This agreement obliges them to resolve any specified disputes through arbitration rather than litigation.

Non-Signatories

In various legal systems, several legal theories can bind entities that have not signed an arbitration agreement. These include piercing the corporate veil, agency (actual and apparent), “group of companies” doctrine, estoppel, succession, third-party beneficiary, guarantors, ratification, assignment, and assumption theories. In each case, non-signatories may be bound by or invoke the arbitration clause within the contract.

Document production

Document production is a procedural tool by which a party or the tribunal can request (and order) the production of documents in possession of the other party.

The IBA Rules of Evidence provide a frequently used procedure for document production in international arbitration. Under the IBA Rules of Evidence, each party discloses the categories of documents relevant to its case or defence in advance.According to Article 3(2) of the IBA Rules of Evidence, the tribunal sets a date by which each party shall request identified categories of documents to be disclosed by the opposing party. Each party must detail the relevance and materiality of its requests and explain why certain categories of documents are relevant to the case and material to its outcome. These requests are typically provided in the form of a Redfern Schedule, including: Requests for production; Justification as to the materiality and relevance of the requests; Reasoned objections, if any, to the requests; and Decision of the arbitral tribunal.

《IBA 证据规则》提供了一种在国际仲裁中经常使用的文件提交程序。根据《IBA 证据规则》，每一方当事人提前披露与其案件相关的文件类别。

根据《IBA 证据规则》第3条第2款，仲裁庭确定每一方当事人应请求对方披露特定类别文件的日期。每一方当事人必须详细说明其请求的相关性和重要性，并解释某些类别的文件为何与案件相关并对其结果有重要影响。这些请求通常以Redfern表的形式提供，包括：文件提交请求；有关请求的重要性和相关性的理由；对请求提出的有理由的反对意见（如有）；以及仲裁庭的决定。

Relevant and Material 相关且重要

In arbitration, “relevant and material” refers to the evidence or information that is both pertinent and significant to the issues being decided.

  • Relevant: Evidence or information that is directly related to the matter at hand and can help establish the facts of the case. 直接与所处理的事项有关，并有助于确定案件事实的证据或信息。
  • Material: Evidence or information that is substantial and has the potential to influence the outcome of the arbitration. It is essential for proving or disproving a point that is in dispute. 实质性的证据或信息，具有可能影响仲裁结果的潜力。它对于证明或反驳争议中的某个关键点是必不可少的。

Arbitrators consider evidence that meets these criteria to make informed and fair decisions.

Costs in Arbitration

International arbitration tribunals generally have the authority to award arbitration costs, including legal fees, to the winning party. Current institutional rules broadly empower tribunals to determine legal costs, with implementation typically based on the party’s success ratio and the reasonableness of their expenses. Most institutional rules recognize arbitrators’ power to ‘apportion’ legal costs between the parties, allowing for awards of less than 100% of one party’s costs. Even if the applicable institutional rules do not expressly grant this power, the arbitration agreement should be interpreted as implicitly granting it. The existence of an implied agreement between the parties authorizing arbitrators to award arbitration costs, including legal fees, is inherent in the tribunal’s authority (unless otherwise agreed).

国际仲裁庭一般有权判给胜诉方仲裁费用，包括法律费用。现行机构规则广泛赋予仲裁庭裁定法律费用的权力，仲裁员通常根据当事人的胜诉比例和费用的合理性来行使这些权力。大多数机构规则承认仲裁员在当事人间“分摊”法律费用的权力，允许判决少于一方当事人费用的100%。即便适用的机构规则没有明确赋予仲裁庭裁决法律费用的权力，仲裁协议应被解释为默示地赋予了这种权力。当事人之间存在默示协议赋权仲裁员裁定仲裁费用，包括法律费用，是仲裁庭权力的题中之意（除非另有约定）。

Interest

In international arbitration, tribunals commonly award interest based on various legal grounds. Many arbitration laws do not provide specific guidelines for arbitrators regarding the award of interest. Consequently, arbitrators frequently consider several factors when determining interest awards:

在国际仲裁中，仲裁庭通常根据各种法律依据裁定利息。许多仲裁法没有为仲裁员提供有关利息裁决的具体指南。因此，仲裁员在确定利息裁决时经常考虑以下几个因素：

  1. Contractual Provisions : Arbitrators often refer to the interest rate specified in the contract. If the parties have agreed upon a particular interest rate in their contract, the tribunal will typically uphold and apply that rate.
    1. 合同条款：仲裁员经常参考合同中规定的利率。如果双方在合同中约定了特定利率，仲裁庭通常会维持并适用该利率。
  2. Commercial Interest Rates : In the absence of a specified rate in the contract, arbitrators may award interest based on commercially prevailing interest rates. These rates reflect what is commonly accepted in the relevant business sector and jurisdiction over the period for which interest is calculated.
    1. 商业利率：如果合同中没有指定利率，仲裁员可以根据商业现行利率裁定利息。这些利率反映了相关商业部门和司法管辖区在利息计算期间普遍接受的利率。
  3. Interest as Damages : Arbitrators may also consider interest as a part of compensatory damages for breach of contract. The rationale is to fully compensate the injured party for financial losses incurred due to the breach, which includes the loss of use of money over time.
    1. 利息作为损害赔偿：仲裁员还可以将利息视为违约损害赔偿的一部分。理由是全额赔偿受害方因违规行为而遭受的经济损失，其中包括随着时间的推移而造成的资金使用损失。
  4. Legal Grounds : Tribunals might also award interest based on statutory or legal principles recognized in the relevant jurisdiction. This approach ensures that the awarded interest aligns with the legal framework governing the dispute.
    1. 法律依据：法庭还可能根据相关司法管辖区认可的法定或法律原则判给利息。这种方法确保所授予的权益符合管辖争议的法律框架。

In summary, when determining interest awards in arbitration, tribunals take into account contractual terms, commercially prevailing rates, compensatory damages considerations, and statutory legal principles to ensure that the awarded interest is fair and reasonable.

综上所述，仲裁庭在确定仲裁利息时，会综合考虑合同条款、商业通行费率、损害赔偿考虑因素以及法定法律原则，以确保裁决的利息公平合理。

Tribunal Secretary

A Tribunal Secretary, also known as an arbitral secretary or administrative secretary, is an individual appointed to assist the arbitration tribunal in managing the procedural and administrative aspects of an arbitration case. The role and functions of a Tribunal Secretary can significantly enhance the efficiency and effectiveness of the arbitration process.

仲裁庭秘书，也称为仲裁秘书或行政秘书，是被任命协助仲裁庭管理仲裁案件的程序和行政方面的人员。仲裁庭秘书的角色和职能可以显着提高仲裁程序的效率和效力。

  • Administrative Support : The Tribunal Secretary handles the logistical and administrative tasks of the arbitration, such as organizing hearings, managing correspondence, and maintaining records.
    • 行政支持：仲裁庭秘书负责处理仲裁的后勤和行政任务，例如组织听证会、管理信件和保存记录。
  • Document Management : The secretary ensures that all documents submitted by the parties are properly organized, distributed, and filed. This includes preparing bundles, indexing documents, and managing exhibits. 文件管理：秘书确保各方提交的所有文件得到妥善组织、分发和归档。这包括准备捆绑包、索引文档和管理展品。
  • Drafting Assistance : While the Tribunal Secretary may assist in drafting procedural orders, summaries, and other non-substantive documents, they must not be involved in drafting the final award or any decisions on the merits of the case. 起草协助：虽然仲裁庭秘书可以协助起草程序令、摘要和其他非实质性文件，但他们不得参与起草最终裁决或任何有关案件实质的决定。
  • Liaison Role : Acting as a point of contact, the Tribunal Secretary facilitates communication between the parties and the tribunal, coordinating scheduling and procedural steps. 联络角色：作为联络点，仲裁庭秘书促进双方和仲裁庭之间的沟通，协调时间安排和程序步骤。

Scope and Limitations:

  • Non-Decision Making : It is crucial that the Tribunal Secretary does not influence or participate in the tribunal’s substantive decision-making. The ultimate responsibility for all decisions lies with the arbitrators. 非决策：仲裁庭秘书不影响或参与仲裁庭的实质性决策至关重要。所有决定的最终责任由仲裁员承担。
  • Transparency : The appointment and role of the Tribunal Secretary should be transparent, with their tasks clearly defined and agreed upon by the parties. 透明度：仲裁庭秘书的任命和角色应透明，其任务应明确界定并得到各方同意。
  • Confidentiality : As with all participants in the arbitration, the Tribunal Secretary must maintain strict confidentiality regarding the arbitration proceedings and related information. 保密：与仲裁的所有参与者一样，仲裁庭秘书必须对仲裁程序和相关信息严格保密。

Typically, the appointment of a Tribunal Secretary requires the consent of both parties to ensure fairness and acceptance of the support provided. 通常，仲裁庭秘书的任命需要双方同意，以确保所提供的支持的公平性和接受性。

Various arbitration institutions have specific rules and guidelines governing the use and role of Tribunal Secretaries, such as the ICC, LCIA, and HKIAC. 各个仲裁机构都有具体的规则和指南来管理仲裁庭秘书的使用和角色，例如国际商会 (ICC)、伦敦国际仲裁院 (LCIA) 和香港国际仲裁中心 (HKIAC)。

In summary, a Tribunal Secretary plays a vital role in supporting the tribunal, helping to streamline the arbitration process, while maintaining strict adherence to their defined scope of duties to ensure the integrity of the arbitration.

总之，仲裁庭秘书在支持仲裁庭、帮助简化仲裁程序、同时严格遵守其规定的职责范围以确保仲裁的公正性方面发挥着至关重要的作用。

Cousel Conduct

In 2013, the IBA issued the Guidelines on Party Representation in International Arbitration (the “IBA Guidelines”). These Guidelines are designed to ensure that party representatives act with integrity and honesty, avoid unnecessary delays and expenses, and refrain from obstructive tactics.The use of the term “guidelines” instead of “rules” emphasizes their contractual nature. The IBA Guidelines are non-binding unless parties mutually agree to their application. Despite their potential limitations and criticisms due to their non-binding nature, they offer practical guidance for resolving ethical dilemmas in arbitration.

During the revision of its 2018 Rules, the Hong Kong International Arbitration Center (HKIAC) Rules Revision Committee discussed the need to include ethical standards for counsel but ultimately chose not to incorporate them explicitly. In Hong Kong, barristers must adhere to the Code of Conduct issued by the Hong Kong Bar Association, and solicitors must follow The Hong Kong Solicitors’ Guide to Professional Conduct issued by the Law Society of Hong Kong. The Committee deemed these existing codes sufficient and did not feel the need for additional ethical obligations in the HKIAC Rules, unlike the London International Court of Arbitration (LCIA).

香港国际仲裁中心（HKIAC）规则修订委员会在修订2018年规则期间讨论了纳入律师道德标准的必要性，但最终选择不明确纳入。在香港，大律师必须遵守香港大律师公会颁布的《行为守则》，事务律师则必须遵守香港律师会颁布的《香港律师专业操守指南》。与伦敦国际仲裁院 (LCIA) 不同，委员会认为这些现有准则已足够，并且认为无需在 HKIAC 规则中规定额外的道德义务。

Validation Principle

The validation principle is an established principle of contractual interpretation. Where there is ambiguity in a contract, the law presumes that the interpretation that upholds the validity of the contract will prevail.

效力原则是合同解释的一个确立原则。当合同中存在歧义时，法律推定应选择那个保持合同有效的解释。

A validation principle looks to the purposes of international arbitration agreements and provides for application of the law that will give effect to the parties’agreement. This principle rests on the premise that parties generally intend application of that law which will give effect to their agreement to arbitrate and provide safeguards against the peculiar jurisdictional and choice-of-law uncertainties of transnational litigation. Notably, and unlike some national law systems, the validation principle is mandated by the New York Convention and the Model Law and applies to all international arbitration agreements, regardless where the arbitral seat is located.

效力原则关注国际仲裁协议的目的，并为适用法律提供依据，以确保当事人的协议得以生效。该原则基于这样一个前提，即当事人通常希望适用能使其仲裁协议生效的法律，并提供防范跨国诉讼中有关管辖权和法律选择的不确定性的保障。值得注意的是，效力原则不同于某些国家的法律体系，效力原则由《纽约公约》和《示范法》所规定，并适用于所有国际仲裁协议，不论仲裁地在哪里。

Jivraj v Hashwani

The dispute in Jivraj v Hashwani centered around an arbitration clause in a joint venture agreement requiring arbitrators to be respected members of the Ismaili community. Mr. Hashwani challenged this requirement under the Employment Equality (Religion and Belief) Regulations 2003.

Jivraj 诉 Hashwani 案的争议围绕合资协议中的仲裁条款展开，该条款要求仲裁员必须是受人尊敬的伊斯玛仪派社区成员。 Hashwani 先生根据 2003 年《就业平等（宗教和信仰）条例》对这一要求提出了质疑。

  • First Instance : David Steel J dismissed the challenge, ruling that arbitrators are not “employees” under the Regulations and, even if they were, the religious requirement was justified under the GOR exception. 一审：David Steel J 驳回了这一质疑，裁定仲裁员不是《条例》中的“雇员”，即使是，宗教要求在 GOR 例外情况下也是合理的。
  • Court of Appeal : Reversed the decision, holding that arbitrators were employees and the religious requirement was not necessary for an English tribunal. 上诉法院：推翻了裁决，认为仲裁员是雇员，并且英国法庭没有必要提出宗教要求。
  • Supreme Court : Overturned the Court of Appeal, concluding that arbitrators are not employees but “quasi-judicial adjudicators” and independent providers of services, thus not subject to the anti-discrimination provisions. 最高法院：推翻了上诉法院，裁定仲裁员不是雇员，而是“准司法裁决者”和独立的服务提供者，因此不受反歧视条款的约束。

The Supreme Court emphasized the importance of the parties’ autonomy in choosing arbitrators, recognizing that specific requirements can ensure trust in the arbitration process. This decision supports the principle that arbitration can tailor the selection of arbitrators based on cultural and personal characteristics relevant to the dispute.

最高法院强调了当事人选择仲裁员自主权的重要性，并认识到具体要求可以确保对仲裁程序的信任。该决定支持仲裁可以根据与争议相关的文化和个人特征来定制仲裁员的选择这一原则。

Arbitrator Agreement

An “Arbitrator Agreement” refers to the contractual arrangement between the parties involved in the arbitration and the appointed arbitrators. This agreement outlines the terms and conditions under which the arbitrators will conduct the arbitration proceedings.

Procedural Order

A procedural order is an instruction or directive issued by the arbitral tribunal to manage the procedural aspects of the arbitration. It can cover a wide range of matters, including timelines for submissions, the schedule of hearings, the exchange of documents, and other procedural steps necessary for the efficient conduct of the arbitration.

Default Award

A default award is rendered by the arbitral tribunal when one party fails to participate in the arbitration process, such as by not attending hearings or not submitting required documents. If the non-participation is without valid reason, the tribunal may proceed and issue an award based on the evidence and submissions of the participating party.

当一方当事人未参加仲裁程序（例如未出席听证会或未提交所需文件）时，仲裁庭会作出缺席裁决。如果无正当理由不参与，仲裁庭可以根据参与方的证据和意见继续进行裁决并作出裁决。

Settlement

Settlement refers to the resolution of a dispute between the parties through mutual agreement, without the need for a formal arbitral award. The parties agree on the terms to resolve the conflict, which can be confirmed in writing and, upon request, incorporated into a consent award by the tribunal.

和解是指当事人之间通过双方协议解决争议，无需正式仲裁裁决。双方就解决冲突的条款达成一致，可以书面形式确认，并根据要求纳入仲裁庭的同意裁决中。

Interim Measure

An interim measure is a temporary order issued by the arbitral tribunal to preserve the status quo, protect assets, or prevent harm or prejudice to the arbitration process. Examples of interim measures include orders to maintain or restore the status quo, preserve evidence, or prevent the removal or dissipation of assets. Interim measures are also known as provisional or conservatory measures.

临时措施是仲裁庭为维持现状、保护资产或防止仲裁程序受到损害或损害而发布的临时命令。临时措施的例子包括维持或恢复现状、保存证据或防止资产转移或耗散的命令。临时措施也称为临时措施或保全措施。

Award

According to both the New York Convention and domestic arbitration laws, a document must meet three essential criteria to be considered an “award” in arbitration:

根据《纽约公约》和国内仲裁法，文件必须满足三个基本标准才能被视为仲裁“裁决”：

(a) The award must be made based on an agreement to “arbitrate” between the parties. This implies that the parties have contractually agreed to settle their disputes through arbitration. 裁决必须根据双方之间的“仲裁”协议作出。这意味着双方已按照合同同意通过仲裁解决争议。

(b) The award must embody the fundamental characteristics inherent in the concept of “award.” This means it should reflect the formal decision and judgment of the arbitral tribunal concerning the matters submitted for arbitration. 裁决必须体现“裁决”概念固有的基本特征。这意味着它应反映仲裁庭对提交仲裁事项的正式决定和判断。

(c) The award must resolve substantive issues of law, not merely procedural issues. This indicates that the decision should address the core legal and factual disputes between the parties, providing a resolution to the core controversy. 裁决必须解决实质性法律问题，而不仅仅是程序问题。这表明该判决应当针对当事人之间的核心法律和事实争议，为核心争议提供解决方案。

Only when these conditions are met can a legal document be considered an award, making it subject to the provisions of the New York Convention and domestic arbitration laws.

只有满足这些条件，法律文件才能被视为裁决，从而受到《纽约公约》和国内仲裁法规定的约束。

Consent Award

In practice, it is not uncommon for parties to reach a settlement agreement during arbitration. If the parties successfully negotiate a resolution to their dispute, they may choose to withdraw from arbitration and record the settlement terms in a contract. Alternatively, the parties may wish to obtain a “consent award” (or “settlement award”) that documents the terms of their settlement.

Security for Costs（费用担保）

Security for costs is a measure used in arbitration where one party is ordered to provide a guarantee or deposit to cover potential costs that the other party may incur. This is typically requested when there is a concern that the claimant may not be able to pay the costs if the arbitration award is unfavorable to them.

费用担保是仲裁中使用的一种措施，要求一方当事人提供担保或押金，以支付另一方可能产生的潜在费用。当担心仲裁裁决对其不利时，申请人可能无法支付费用时，通常会提出这一请求。

Partial Award（部分裁决）

A “partial award” refers to an arbitral decision that definitively addresses some, but not all, of the parties’ claims in arbitration, leaving the remaining claims to be considered and resolved in subsequent arbitration proceedings. For the claims addressed in such an award, the partial award may become a “final” award and be binding on the parties. It may also be recognized and enforced (or set aside).

Discretionary Power

Discretionary power refers to the authority granted to arbitrators to make decisions based on their judgment and experience. This power allows arbitrators flexibility in determining procedural and substantive matters to ensure fair and efficient resolution of the dispute.

自由裁量权是指授予仲裁员根据其判断和经验做出决定的权力。这一权力使仲裁员可以灵活地确定程序和实质性事项，以确保公平有效地解决争议。

Waiver of Right to Recourse Against an Award（放弃对裁决的追索权）

There is a trend where some arbitral institutions’ rules allow for the waiver of the rights of recourse against an arbitral award. These rights of recourse are typically found in articles 34 and 36 of the UNCITRAL Model Law, rooted in Article V of the New York Convention. Article 34 allows applications to set aside an award to be made to the court at the seat of arbitration, while Article 36 permits requests to refuse recognition and enforcement of an award to be made in any court where enforcement is sought.

目前有一种趋势，一些仲裁机构的规则允许放弃对仲裁裁决的追索权。这些追索权通常在《联合国国际贸易法委员会仲裁示范法》（UNCITRAL Model Law）的第34和36条中找到，其基础是《纽约公约》第五条。第34条允许向仲裁地法院提出撤销仲裁裁决的申请，而第36条允许在任何寻求执行的法院提出拒绝承认和执行仲裁裁决的请求。

The UNCITRAL Arbitration Rules (revised in 2010) introduced the concept of waiver clauses, suggesting that parties could agree to waive their rights of recourse against an award to any court or other competent authority, provided that such a waiver is valid under the applicable law. This clause serves as a model and has been adopted and modified by many arbitral institutions.

2010年修订的《联合国国际贸易法委员会仲裁规则》（UNCITRAL Arbitration Rules）引入了放弃条款的概念，建议当事人可以同意放弃他们对任何法院或其他有权机关对裁决的追索权，只要这种放弃在适用法律下是有效的。该条款作为一个模型，并已被许多仲裁机构采纳和修改。

Institutions like the ICC, LCIA, SIAC, and others have incorporated waiver clauses into their arbitration rules. For instance, Article 35(6) of the ICC Rules and Article 26.8 of the LCIA Rules state that by agreeing to arbitration under these rules, parties waive their rights to recourse against the award as long as such a waiver is not prohibited by applicable law. These clauses help arbitral institutions to gain a competitive edge but raise public policy concerns regarding the validity and notice of such waivers in the parties’ agreements.

像ICC、LCIA、SIAC等机构已经在其仲裁规则中纳入了放弃条款。例如，ICC规则第35(6)条和LCIA规则第26.8条规定，通过同意根据这些规则进行仲裁，当事人放弃对裁决的追索权，只要这种放弃不受适用法律的禁止。这些条款帮助仲裁机构获得竞争优势，但也引起了关于公共政策的担忧，即在当事人协议中，这种放弃的有效性和通知程度问题。

Mediation

Mediation is a voluntary and confidential process where a neutral third party, called a mediator, facilitates negotiations between disputing parties to help them reach a mutually agreeable solution. The mediator does not impose a decision but assists the parties in finding common ground.：

调解是一个自愿和保密的过程，中立的第三方（称为调解员）促进争议双方之间的谈判，帮助他们达成双方都同意的解决方案。调解员并不强加决定，而是协助各方找到共同点。

Conciliation

Conciliation is a process similar to mediation, involving a neutral third party who helps the disputing parties to resolve their conflict by suggesting possible solutions. The conciliator may take a more active role than a mediator in proposing terms for settlement.

调解是一个类似于调解的过程，涉及中立的第三方，通过提出可能的解决方案来帮助争议各方解决冲突。在提出和解条款方面，调解员可能比调解员发挥更积极的作用。

Negotiation

Negotiation is a direct dialogue between parties to a dispute, aiming to reach a common agreement or resolve the issue without the involvement of third parties. Negotiation involves discussions, compromises, and arrangements made voluntarily by the parties.

谈判是争端各方之间的直接对话，旨在在没有第三方参与的情况下达成共同协议或解决问题。谈判是双方自愿做出的讨论、妥协和安排。

Litigation

Litigation is the process of taking legal action and resolving disputes through the court system. It is generally more formal and rigid, involving judges, attorneys, and adherence to procedural laws and rules.

诉讼是通过法院系统采取法律行动并解决争议的过程。它通常更加正式和严格，涉及法官、律师，并遵守程序法和规则。

Arb-Med-Arb Protocol（仲裁-调解-仲裁程序）:

The Arb-Med-Arb protocol refers to a hybrid dispute resolution process where arbitration proceedings are paused to attempt mediation. If the mediation is successful, the mediated settlement is formalized in a consent award. If the mediation fails, the arbitration resumes, and a final award is rendered by the tribunal.

Arb-Med-Arb 协议是指暂停仲裁程序以尝试调解的混合争议解决流程。如果调解成功，调解和解将以同意书的形式正式确定。如果调解失败，则恢复仲裁，并由仲裁庭作出最终裁决。

Orfs (Outcome Related Fee Structures 结果关联费用结构）

Outcome Related Fee Structures, or ORFS, are arrangements where legal fees are contingent upon the outcome of the case. This structure includes conditional fees, where fees depend partly on the outcome, and success fees, where a lawyer’s remuneration is tied to the success of the client’s case.

结果相关费用结构（ORFS）是法律费用取决于案件结果的安排。这种结构包括按条件收费（收费部分取决于结果）和成功收费（律师的报酬与客户案件的成功挂钩）。

Third Party Funding

Third party funding refers to financial support provided by an outside entity (third party) to a party involved in arbitration. The third party covers the arbitration costs in exchange for a portion of any monetary award or settlement achieved. This arrangement helps parties with limited financial resources pursue their claims.

第三方资助是指外部实体（第三方）向仲裁当事人提供的资金支持。第三方承担仲裁费用，以换取所达成的任何金钱裁决或和解的一部分。这种安排有助于财力有限的当事人寻求索赔。

UNCITRAL Model Law

The UNCITRAL Model Law on International Commercial Arbitration is a template of laws designed by the United Nations Commission on International Trade Law (UNCITRAL) to help countries harmonize their arbitration laws. It provides a comprehensive legal framework for the conduct of international commercial arbitration.

《贸易法委员会国际商事仲裁示范法》是联合国国际贸易法委员会（贸易法委员会）为帮助各国协调其仲裁法而设计的法律模板。它为国际商事仲裁的进行提供了全面的法律框架。

Multi-Tier Arbitration Clause

A multi-tier arbitration clause requires parties to engage in one or more preliminary steps, such as negotiation or mediation, before initiating formal arbitration proceedings. This approach aims to resolve disputes amicably before resorting to arbitration.

多层仲裁条款要求当事人在启动正式仲裁程序之前进行一项或多项初步步骤，例如谈判或调解。这种做法旨在在诉诸仲裁之前友好解决争议。

Friendly Negotiations

Friendly negotiations refer to informal discussions between disputing parties aimed at reaching a mutually acceptable resolution. This process fosters open communication and cooperation, reducing the need for formal dispute resolution mechanisms.

友好谈判是指争议双方进行非正式讨论，以达成双方都能接受的解决方案。这一过程促进了开放的沟通与合作，减少了对正式争议解决机制的需求。

Pathological Arbitration Clause

A pathological arbitration clause is a defective or poorly drafted arbitration agreement that creates ambiguity or inconsistency in how arbitration should be conducted. These flaws can lead to disputes over the clause’s interpretation and enforceability.

病态仲裁条款是指有缺陷或起草不当的仲裁协议，导致仲裁的进行方式含糊或不一致。这些缺陷可能会导致对该条款的解释和可执行性产生争议。

Inoperable or Incapable of Being Performed

This term refers to situations where an arbitration agreement cannot be executed due to legal or practical reasons, such as the unavailability of named arbitrators or invalidity of the agreement. It renders the arbitration clause ineffective.

本术语是指因无法指定仲裁员或协议无效等法律或实际原因导致仲裁协议无法执行的情况。从而导致仲裁条款无效。

Jurisdictional Challenge

A jurisdictional challenge is an objection raised by a party to dispute the arbitral tribunal’s authority to hear and decide a case. The challenging party argues that the tribunal lacks jurisdiction based on the arbitration agreement or applicable laws.

管辖权质疑是当事人对仲裁庭审理和裁决案件的权力提出的异议。异议方辩称，根据仲裁协议或适用的法律，仲裁庭缺乏管辖权。

Seat of Arbitration

The seat of arbitration is the legal jurisdiction where the arbitration is formally based. It determines the legal framework governing the arbitration proceedings and the extent of court intervention.

仲裁地是仲裁正式所在地的法律管辖区。它决定了管辖仲裁程序的法律框架和法院干预的程度。

Place of Arbitration

The place of arbitration refers to the physical location where arbitration hearings and meetings take place. It can differ from the seat of arbitration and does not necessarily determine the legal framework applicable to the arbitration.

仲裁地点是指仲裁听证会和会议举行的实际地点。它可能与仲裁地不同，并不一定决定适用于仲裁的法律框架。

Arbitration Venue

The arbitration venue is the specific location or facility where arbitration proceedings are conducted. It provides the setting for hearings, meetings, and other procedural activities.

仲裁地点是进行仲裁程序的具体地点或设施。它为听证会、会议和其他程序活动提供了场所。

Arbitral Tribunal

The arbitral tribunal is the panel of one or more arbitrators appointed to hear and resolve a dispute in arbitration. The tribunal conducts the proceedings, evaluates evidence, and renders binding decisions.

仲裁庭是由一名或多名仲裁员组成的小组，被指定在仲裁中审理并解决争议。仲裁庭进行诉讼、评估证据并做出具有约束力的决定。

Dissenting Opinion

A dissenting opinion is a separate statement written by a member of the arbitral tribunal who disagrees with the majority decision. The dissenting arbitrator presents their reasoning and alternative view on the case.

异议意见是仲裁庭成员不同意多数决定的单独声明。持异议的仲裁员提出了他们对案件的推理和替代观点。

Remedy

A remedy is the relief or compensation sought by a party in arbitration to address a legal injury or breach of contract. Remedies can include monetary compensation, specific performance, or declaratory relief.

补救措施是仲裁一方为解决法律损害或违约而寻求的救济或赔偿。补救措施可以包括金钱补偿、具体绩效或声明性救济。

Relief Sought

Relief sought refers to the specific remedies or outcomes that a party requests from the arbitral tribunal. It outlines the resolution the party seeks for its claims and disputes.

寻求救济是指当事人向仲裁庭请求的具体补救措施或结果。它概述了该方为其索赔和争议寻求的解决方案。

Counterclaim（反诉）

A counterclaim is a claim made by the respondent against the claimant in arbitration. It allows the respondent to assert its own claims and seek relief within the same arbitration proceeding.

反诉是被申请人在仲裁中向申请人提出的请求。它允许被申请人在同一仲裁程序中主张自己的主张并寻求救济。

Reasonable Opportunity to Present a Case

This principle ensures that all parties in arbitration are given a fair and equal opportunity to present their arguments, evidence, and defenses. It upholds the principles of due process and procedural fairness.

这一原则确保仲裁中的所有当事人都有公平、平等的机会提出自己的论点、证据和抗辩。它坚持正当程序和程序公平的原则。

Lex Arbitri（仲裁法）

Lex arbitri refers to the set of laws governing the arbitration process, typically based on the legal framework of the seat of arbitration. It determines procedural issues such as the appointment of arbitrators, conduct of hearings, and recourse against awards.

仲裁法是指管辖仲裁程序的一套法律，通常基于仲裁地的法律框架。它决定仲裁员的任命、听证会的进行以及对裁决的追索等程序问题。

Lex Loci Arbitri（仲裁地法）

Lex loci arbitri refers to the law of the place where the arbitration is held. It can influence procedural aspects of arbitration and the level of court support available for the arbitration process.

仲裁地法是指仲裁地的法律。它可以影响仲裁的程序方面以及法院对仲裁过程的支持水平。

Lex loci arbitri is the Latin term for “the law of the place where arbitration is to occur” in the context of conflict of laws. The fundamental basis for arbitration is referred to as lex arbitri, which is the law governing arbitration. The seat of arbitration is sometimes also called Lex Arbitri. The lex loci arbitri is of critical importance to the seat of arbitration because it is the courts of the seat that have supervisory authority over the arbitral process.

Lex loci arbitri 是拉丁语术语，在法律冲突的情况下表示“仲裁发生地的法律”。仲裁的基本依据称为仲裁法，即管辖仲裁的法律。仲裁地有时也称为 Lex Arbitri。仲裁地法对于仲裁地至关重要，因为仲裁地法院对仲裁程序拥有监督权。

“The law of the place where arbitration is to occur” refers to the arbitration law applicable in the location chosen by the parties as the “seat of arbitration.” This means that the legal framework governing the arbitration proceedings will be defined by the jurisdiction of the chosen seat.

是的，“仲裁地法律”是指当事人选择的“仲裁地”所在地适用的仲裁法。这意味着管辖仲裁程序的法律框架将由所选所在地的管辖区确定。

Exhaustive List

An exhaustive list is a comprehensive and complete enumeration of items, factors, or elements.

详尽的列表是对项目、因素或元素的全面且完整的列举。

In the context of the UNCITRAL Model Law and the New York Convention, an exhaustive list is provided for the grounds on which the enforcement of an arbitral award can be refused. This means that only the specific exceptions listed in Article 36 of the UNCITRAL Model Law and Article V of the New York Convention can be used as valid reasons to refuse enforcement. No other grounds, including national laws or a review of the merits of the award, are allowed to be considered. This ensures that the list is exclusive and limited to the most serious irregularities.

在《贸易法委员会示范法》和《纽约公约》的背景下，提供了拒绝执行仲裁裁决的理由的详尽清单。这意味着，只有《贸易法委员会示范法》第36条和《纽约公约》第五条中列出的特定例外情况可以作为拒绝执行的有效理由。不能考虑其他理由，包括国家法律或对裁决的是非曲直的审查。这确保了该列表是排他性的，并且仅限于最严重的不规范行为。
